/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PRC_ColorMaster]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[PRC_ColorMaster]
@Type nvarchar(50),
@ColorName nvarchar(50)=null,
@ColorRowId bigint=null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50)=null
AS
BEGIN
   IF @Type='SELECT'
     BEGIN
		  SELECT [RowID]
		        ,[ColorName]
			    ,[CreatedBy]
		   	    ,[CreatedOn]
		  FROM [dbo].[ColorMaster] Order By ColorName
	 END
   ELSE IF (@TYPE = 'SEARCH')
		BEGIN
			  SELECT [RowID]
		            ,[COLORNAME]
				    ,[CREATEDBY]
				    ,CONVERT(VARCHAR(10),CREATEDON,103) [CREATEDON]
			  FROM [DBO].[COLORMASTER]
			  WHERE [COLORNAME] LIKE '%' + @COLORNAME + '%'
		END
	ELSE IF(@TYPE='SELECTBYID')
	  BEGIN
	       SELECT [RowID]
		         ,[COLORNAME]
				 ,[CREATEDBY]
				 ,CONVERT(VARCHAR(10),CREATEDON,103) [CREATEDON]
		    FROM [DBO].[COLORMASTER] 
			WHERE [COLORNAME] = @COLORNAME
		
	  END
   ELSE IF @Type='INSERT'
      BEGIN
	     INSERT INTO [dbo].[ColorMaster]
           ([ColorName]
           ,[CreatedBy]
           ,[CreatedOn])
         VALUES
           (@ColorName
           ,@CreatedBy
           ,GETDATE())
	  END
   ELSE IF @Type='UPDATE'
      BEGIN
	     UPDATE [dbo].[ColorMaster]
		 SET    [ColorName] = @ColorName
		 WHERE  RowID=@ColorRowId
	  END
   ELSE IF @Type='DELETE'
      BEGIN
	     DELETE [dbo].[ColorMaster]
		 WHERE  RowID=@ColorRowId
	  END
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_CustomerMaster]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_CustomerMaster] 
@Type varchar(max),
@Name nvarchar(50)=null,
@Address nvarchar(250)=null,
@Location nvarchar(100)=null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50)=null

AS
BEGIN
	Declare @Count int;
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			SELECT CustomerName,Address,Location,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM CustomerMaster ORDER BY CustomerName
		end
	else if (@Type = 'SEARCH')
		begin
			SELECT CustomerName,Address,Location,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM CustomerMaster
			WHERE CustomerName like '%' + @Name + '%'
		end
	else if(@Type='SELECTBYID')
	  begin
		SELECT CustomerName,Address,Location,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM CustomerMaster
		WHERE CustomerName = @Name
	  end
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
	    INSERT INTO [dbo].CustomerMaster
           (CustomerName
           ,Address
		   ,Location
           ,[CreatedOn]
           ,[CreatedBy])
		 VALUES
           (@Name
           ,@Address
		   ,@Location
           ,GETDATE()
           ,@CreatedBy)

			Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	 else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	  begin
	     UPDATE [dbo].CustomerMaster
		   SET Address = @Address
		 WHERE CustomerName = @Name and Location=@Location
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	  begin
	     delete from dbo.CustomerMaster WHERE CustomerName = @Name and Location=@Location
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_CustomerReturn]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_CustomerReturn]
(
	@Type varchar(max),@DispatcDate datetime,@ModelNo varchar(50)=null,@CustomerId numeric(18,0)=null,
	@DispatchOrderId numeric(18,0)=null,@TrolleyNo varchar(50)=null,@Qty int=null,@SelectedModel varchar(50)=null,
	@Reason varchar(500)=null,@UserId varchar(50)=null,@FinalPackStatus int=null,@TrolleyStatus int=null
)
AS
BEGIN
	/*
		Note: There is not much difference between dispatch cancel and customer return, except in case of customer return
		dispatch order qty will not be decreased and dispatch order will be treated as partial close as dispatch qty will be 
		more than actual dispatch qty
	*/
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
	Begin
		Select 'False' As [Select],DD.DispatchOrderId,(Cm.CustomerName+'-'+CM.Location) As Customer,DD.ModelNo,
		DD.TrolleyNo,Sum(DD.Qty) As DispatchQty
		 From DispatchOrder DO Join DispatchDetail DD On DO.Id = DD.DispatchOrderId
		 Join CustomerMaster CM On Do.CustomerId = CM.Id
		 Where DO.DispatchDate = @DispatcDate And DO.ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' 
		And Do.CustomerId = (Case When @CustomerId = 0 Then DO.CustomerId Else @CustomerId End) 
		 Group By DD.DispatchOrderId, (Cm.CustomerName+'-'+CM.Location),DD.ModelNo,DD.TrolleyNo
		Order By Customer,ModelNo
	End
	Else If(@Type='DELETE')
	Begin
		--Update Trolley status in final packing
		Update FinalPacking Set Status = @FinalPackStatus Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
		And MachiningTrolleyCard In (Select MachiningTrolleyCard From DispatchDetail Where DispatchOrderId = @DispatchOrderId And TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo )
		--Insert data in dispatch deleted table# data will come from dispatch details table
		INSERT INTO [dbo].[DispatchDetail_Deleted]([DispatchOrderId],[Shift],[ModelNo],[TrolleyNo]
        ,[LotNo],[LotNoDate],[MachiningTrolleyCard],[Qty],[DispatchOn],[DispatchBy],[DeleteOn],[DeleteBy],[DeleteReason])
		Select DispatchOrderId,[Shift],ModelNo,TrolleyNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,MachiningTrolleyCard
		,Qty,DispatchOn,DispatchBy,GETDATE(),@UserId,@Reason From DispatchDetail 
		Where DispatchOrderId = @DispatchOrderId And TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
		--Now Delete From Dispatch Details table
		Delete From DispatchDetail Where DispatchOrderId = @DispatchOrderId And TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo 
		--Update Partial status
		Update DispatchOrder Set IsPartialClose = 1,PartialCloseReason = @Reason Where Id = @DispatchOrderId 
		--Update TrolleyStatus
		Update TrolleyMaster Set Status = @TrolleyStatus Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
			
		Select 'Y' As Result
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Delete_TrolleyCard]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Delete_TrolleyCard]
(
	@Type varchar(max),@Process varchar(50) = NULL,@TrolleyCard varchar(50) = NULL,@TrolleyNo varchar(50)= NULL
	,@Reason varchar(250) = NULL,@UserId varchar(50)= NULL
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	If(@Type = 'SELECT')
	Begin
		Declare @CardStatus int = 0,@Qty int = 0,@ChargeNo int,@PalletNo int,@LotNoDate date,@Line_No varchar(50)
		If(@Process = 'CUTTING')
		Begin
			Select @CardStatus = Status,@Qty = (Sum(OkQty) - (Sum(QASampleQty)+Sum(QAPartialNgQty))) ,
			@ChargeNo = ChargeNo,@PalletNo = PalletNo,@LotNoDate = LotNoDate,@Line_No = Line_No From Cutting 
			Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard Group By Status,ChargeNo,PalletNo,LotNoDate,Line_No
			If(@CardStatus = 0)
			Begin
				Select 'Wrong Trolley Card' As Result
				Return
			End
			If(@CardStatus > 5)
			Begin
				Select 'Card has moved to picking/machining, so you can not delete it now.' As Result
				Return
			End
			-- to delete the cutting trolley card,it should be last trolley card for charge and pallet
			If Exists(Select * From Cutting Where LotNoDate = @LotNoDate And Line_No = @Line_No And ChargeNo > @ChargeNo)
			Begin
				Select 'For this trolley card lot no date there is greater charge no than this, so you can not delete' As Result
				Return
			End
			If Exists(Select * From Cutting Where LotNoDate = @LotNoDate And Line_No = @Line_No And ChargeNo = @ChargeNo And PalletNo > @PalletNo)
			Begin
				Select 'For this trolley card lot no date there is greater pallet no than this, so you can not delete' As Result
				Return
			End
			Select 'Y' As Result,@Qty As Qty
		End
		Else If(@Process = 'MACHINING')
		Begin
			
			Select @CardStatus = Status,@Qty = Sum(OkQty) From Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard Group By Status
			If(@CardStatus = 0)
			Begin
				Select 'Wrong Trolley Card' As Result
				Return
			End
			If(@CardStatus = 2)
			Begin
				Select 'Packing already done, so you can not delete it now.' As Result
				Return
			End
			
			Select 'Y' As Result,@Qty As Qty
		End
		Else If(@Process = 'FINAL_PACKING')
		Begin
			Set @Qty = 0
			Select @Qty = IsNull(Sum(OkQty),0) From FinalPacking Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And Status = 1
			If(@Qty = 0)
			Begin
				Select 'Wrong Trolley or trolley has dispatched, so you can not delete now.' As Result
				Return
			End
			
			Select 'Y' As Result,@Qty As Qty
		End
	End
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	Begin
		Begin Try
		Begin Tran
			If(@Process = 'CUTTING')
			Begin
				--Insert into history before deletion
				INSERT INTO [dbo].[DeleteHistory] ([ModelNo],LotNo ,[TrolleyCard] ,[OkQty] ,[Reason] ,[Process] 
				,[DeleteOn] ,[DeleteBy]) 
				Select ModelNo,LotNo ,TrolleyCard ,OkQty ,@Reason ,@Process ,GETDATE() ,@UserId From Cutting Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
				--Now delete the data
				Delete From Cutting Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
			End
			Else If(@Process = 'MACHINING')
			Begin
				--Insert into history before deletion
				INSERT INTO [dbo].[DeleteHistory] ([ModelNo],LotNo ,[TrolleyCard] ,[OkQty] ,[Reason] ,[Process] 
				,[DeleteOn] ,[DeleteBy]) 
				Select ModelNo,LotNo ,TrolleyCard ,OkQty ,@Reason ,@Process ,GETDATE() ,@UserId From Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
				--Update Cutting
				Update Cutting Set Status = 2 Where TrolleyCard = (Select CuttingTrolleyCard From Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard)
				--Now delete the data
				Delete From Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
			End
			Else If(@Process = 'FINAL_PACKING')
			Begin
				--Insert into history before deletion
				INSERT INTO [dbo].[DeleteHistory] ([ModelNo],LotNo ,[TrolleyCard] ,[OkQty],NgQty ,[Reason] ,[Process],TrolleyNo 
				,[DeleteOn] ,[DeleteBy]) 
				Select ModelNo,LotNo ,MachiningTrolleyCard ,OkQty,NgQty ,@Reason ,@Process,TrolleyNo ,GETDATE() ,@UserId From FinalPacking Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And Status = 1
				--Update Machining
				Update Ma Set Ma.FinalPackQty = Ma.FinalPackQty - (Fp.OkQty + Fp.NgQty) From Machining Ma Join FinalPacking FP On Ma.TrolleyCard = Fp.MachiningTrolleyCard 
				And Ma.ModelNo = Fp.ModelNo And Ma.LotNo = Fp.LotNo Where Fp.TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And Fp.Status = 1
				--Update Machining Status
				Update Machining Set Status = 1 Where TrolleyCard In (Select MachiningTrolleyCard From FinalPacking Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And Status = 1)
				And OkQty  > FinalPackQty
			
				--Updat Trolley
				Update TrolleyMaster Set PackQty = PackQty - (Select Sum(OkQty) From FinalPacking Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And Status = 1) Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
				--Update Trolley Status
				Update TrolleyMaster Set IsEmpty = 'True' Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo 
				
				--Now delete the data
				Delete From FinalPacking Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And Status=1
			End
		Commit Tran
		Select 'Y' As Result
		End Try
		Begin Catch
			RollBack Tran
			DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000);  
			DECLARE @ErrorSeverity INT;  
			DECLARE @ErrorState INT;  
  
			SELECT   
			@ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),  
			@ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),  
			@ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();  
   
			RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, -- Message text.  
				@ErrorSeverity, -- Severity.  
				@ErrorState -- State.  
				);
		End Catch
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Dispatch_Cancel]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Dispatch_Cancel]
(
	@Type varchar(max),@DispatcDate datetime,@ModelNo varchar(50)=null,@CustomerId numeric(18,0)=null,
	@DispatchOrderId numeric(18,0)=null,@TrolleyNo varchar(50)=null,@Qty int=null,@SelectedModel varchar(50)=null,
	@Reason varchar(500)=null,@UserId varchar(50)=null,@FinalPackStatus int=null,@TrolleyStatus int=null
)
AS
BEGIN
	
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
	Begin
		Select 'False' As [Select],DD.DispatchOrderId,(Cm.CustomerName+'-'+CM.Location) As Customer,DD.ModelNo,
		DD.TrolleyNo,Sum(DD.Qty) As DispatchQty
		 From DispatchOrder DO Join DispatchDetail DD On DO.Id = DD.DispatchOrderId
		 Join CustomerMaster CM On Do.CustomerId = CM.Id
		 Where DO.DispatchDate = @DispatcDate And DO.ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' 
		And Do.CustomerId = (Case When @CustomerId = 0 Then DO.CustomerId Else @CustomerId End) 
		 Group By DD.DispatchOrderId, (Cm.CustomerName+'-'+CM.Location),DD.ModelNo,DD.TrolleyNo
		Order By Customer,ModelNo
	End
	Else If(@Type='DELETE')
	Begin
		--Update Trolley status in final packing
		Update FinalPacking Set Status = @FinalPackStatus Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
		And MachiningTrolleyCard In (Select MachiningTrolleyCard From DispatchDetail Where DispatchOrderId = @DispatchOrderId And TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo )
		--Insert data in dispatch deleted table# data will come from dispatch details table
		INSERT INTO [dbo].[DispatchDetail_Deleted]([DispatchOrderId],[Shift],[ModelNo],[TrolleyNo]
        ,[LotNo],[LotNoDate],[MachiningTrolleyCard],[Qty],[DispatchOn],[DispatchBy],[DeleteOn],[DeleteBy],[DeleteReason])
		Select DispatchOrderId,[Shift],ModelNo,TrolleyNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,MachiningTrolleyCard
		,Qty,DispatchOn,DispatchBy,GETDATE(),@UserId,@Reason From DispatchDetail 
		Where DispatchOrderId = @DispatchOrderId And TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
		--Now Delete From Dispatch Details table
		Delete From DispatchDetail Where DispatchOrderId = @DispatchOrderId And TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo 
		--Update Dispatch order qty
		Update DispatchOrder Set DispatchQty = DispatchQty - @Qty Where Id = @DispatchOrderId And DispatchQty >= @Qty
		--Remove reserve qty as it has dispatch now 
		Update DispatchReservedQty Set ReservedQty = ReservedQty + @Qty Where ModelNo = @SelectedModel
		--Update TrolleyStatus
		Update TrolleyMaster Set Status = @TrolleyStatus Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
			
		Select 'Y' As Result
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_DispatchOrder]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_DispatchOrder] 
@Type varchar(max),
@Shift nvarchar(50) = null,
@SrNo int =null,@DispatchOrderNo varchar(50)=null,
@DispatchDate nvarchar(50) = null,
@ModelNo nvarchar(50) = null,
@CustomerId nvarchar(50) = null,
@CustomerName nvarchar(50) = null,
@Qty int = null,
@OldQty int = null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50) = null

AS
BEGIN
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			SELECT DispatchOrderNo,CONVERT(varchar(10),DispatchDate,103) DispatchDate,ModelNo,(CustomerName+'-'+Location) As Customer,CustomerId,Qty,DispatchQty,DispatchOrder.CreatedBy
			FROM DispatchOrder Join CustomerMaster On DispatchOrder.CustomerId = CustomerMaster.Id Where Qty > DispatchQty Or DispatchDate=Cast(GETDATE() As Date)
			ORDER BY DispatchDate,CustomerName,Location,ModelNo
		end
	else if (@Type = 'SEARCH')
		begin
			SELECT DispatchOrderNo,CONVERT(varchar(10),DispatchDate,103) DispatchDate,ModelNo,(CustomerName+'-'+Location) As Customer,CustomerId,Qty,DispatchQty,DispatchOrder.CreatedBy
			FROM DispatchOrder Join CustomerMaster On DispatchOrder.CustomerId = CustomerMaster.Id 
			Where DispatchDate = @DispatchDate And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%'
			And CustomerId = (Case When @CustomerId = 0 Then CustomerId Else @CustomerId End) 
			ORDER BY DispatchDate,CustomerName,Location,ModelNo
		end
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
			INSERT INTO [dbo].[DispatchOrder]([Shift],SrNo,DispatchOrderNo,[DispatchDate],[ModelNo],CustomerId
           ,[Qty],[CreatedOn],[CreatedBy])
			VALUES(@Shift,@SrNo,@DispatchOrderNo,@DispatchDate,@ModelNo,@CustomerId,@Qty,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy)
			--Now save qty temporary so that later we can show pending qty
			If Exists(Select ModelNo From DispatchReservedQty Where ModelNo = @ModelNo)
			Begin
				Update DispatchReservedQty Set ReservedQty = ReservedQty + @Qty Where ModelNo = @ModelNo
			End
			Else
			Begin
				INSERT INTO [dbo].[DispatchReservedQty]([ModelNo],[ReservedQty])
				VALUES(@ModelNo,@Qty)
			End

			Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	 else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	  begin
		UPDATE [dbo].[DispatchOrder] SET [Qty] = @Qty,DispatchDate = @DispatchDate,CustomerId = @CustomerId
		 WHERE DispatchOrderNo = @DispatchOrderNo
		 --update qty in reserve qty
		 --New Qty is greater than old qty means qty increase
		 If(@Qty > @OldQty)
		 Begin
			--ADD THE INCREASED QTY
			 Update DispatchReservedQty Set ReservedQty = ReservedQty + (@Qty - @OldQty) Where ModelNo = @ModelNo
		 End
		  --New Qty is less than old qty means qty decrease
		 Else If(@OldQty > @Qty)
		 Begin
			--ADD THE INCREASED QTY
			 Update DispatchReservedQty Set ReservedQty = ReservedQty - (@OldQty - @Qty) Where ModelNo = @ModelNo
		 End
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	  begin
		--Delete only if no dispatch started
		If not exists(Select ModelNo from dbo.DispatchOrder WHERE DispatchOrderNo = @DispatchOrderNo And ISNULL(DispatchQty,0) > 0)
		Begin
			 Delete from dbo.DispatchOrder WHERE DispatchOrderNo = @DispatchOrderNo
			 Update DispatchReservedQty Set ReservedQty = ReservedQty - @Qty Where ModelNo = @ModelNo
			 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
		End
		Else
		Begin
			Select 'Could not delete,dispatch already started' AS RESULT
		End
	  end
END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Get_FinalPacking_Data]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_Get_FinalPacking_Data] 
@TrolleyCard nvarchar(50) = null,@TrolleyNo varchar(50) = null

AS
BEGIN
	--Validate Trolley No
	If Exists(Select TrolleyNo From TrolleyMaster Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo)
	Begin
		Declare @FifoTrolleyCard varchar(50) = ''
		Declare @CardStatus int = 0,@Qty int,@ModelNo varchar(50),@MachineDate date,@ReOilingDate date = NULL
		Declare @IsHold bit = 0
		Select @CardStatus = Status,@Qty = Sum(OkQty),@ModelNo = ModelNo,@ReOilingDate = Cast(ReOilingDate As Date) 
		,@MachineDate = Cast(PrintOn As Date),@IsHold = IsHold From Machining 
		Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And Status = 1 Group By Status,ModelNo,Cast(ReOilingDate As Date),
		Cast(PrintOn As Date),IsHold
		If(@CardStatus = 0)
		Begin
			Select 'Wrong Trolley Card Or Packing already done' As Result
			return
		End
		--If after machining is on hold
		If(@IsHold = 1)
		Begin
			Select 'After machining trolley is on hold,packing is not allowed' As Result
			return
		End
		If(@CardStatus = 1)
		Begin
			-- If reoiling pending then need to check reoiling due date 
			If(@ReOilingDate IS NULL)
			Begin
				Declare @MonthInterVal int
				--Get Month Interval
				Select @MonthInterVal = Month_InterVal From ReOiling_Month
				--If Today date is after or on Reoiling date then return data
				Declare @DueDate date = DATEADD(M,@MonthInterVal,@MachineDate)
				--If trolley is due for reoiling
				if(Cast(GETDATE() As Date) >= @DueDate)
				Begin
					Select 'Trolley is due for reoiling, Machining date is ' + Convert(varchar,@MachineDate,103) + ' and reoiling date is '+ Convert(varchar,@DueDate,103) As Result
				End
				Else
				Begin
					-- fifo should allow previous 2 days date
					SELECT Top(1) @FifoTrolleyCard = TrolleyCard FROM Machining Where LotNoDate <
					(
						SELECT Top(1) DaTEADD(d,-2,LotNoDate) FROM Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard  Order By LotNoDate
					) And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status = 1 And IsHold = 'False'
					 Order By LotNoDate

					--SELECT Top(1) @FifoTrolleyCard = TrolleyCard FROM Machining Where Cast(PrintOn as date) <
					--(
					--	SELECT Top(1) Cast(PrintOn as date) FROM Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard  Order By Cast(PrintOn as date)
					--) And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status = 1 And IsHold = 'False'
					-- Order By Cast(PrintOn as date)


					If(@FifoTrolleyCard = '' Or @FifoTrolleyCard =  NULL)
					Begin
						SELECT DISTINCT 'Y' As Result,ModelNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,(OkQty - (ReOilingNgQty + FinalPackQty + QANgQty)) As Qty
						FROM Machining where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And (OkQty - (ReOilingNgQty + FinalPackQty + QANgQty)) > 0
					
					End
					Else
					Begin
						Select 'As per FIFO you have to scan '+ @FifoTrolleyCard + ' trolley card' As Result
					End
				End
			End
			Else -- if reoiling done then check other condition
			Begin
				--If Scanned trolley card is valid then check FIFO
				-- fifo should allow previous 2 days date
				SELECT Top(1) @FifoTrolleyCard = TrolleyCard FROM Machining Where LotNoDate <
				(
					SELECT Top(1) DaTEADD(d,-2,LotNoDate) FROM Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard  Order By LotNoDate
				) And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status = 1 And IsHold = 'False'
				Order By LotNoDate

				--SELECT Top(1) @FifoTrolleyCard = TrolleyCard FROM Machining Where Cast(PrintOn as date) <
				--(
				--	SELECT Top(1) Cast(PrintOn as date) FROM Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard  Order By Cast(PrintOn as date)
				--) And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status = 1 And IsHold = 'False'
				--Order By Cast(PrintOn as date)

				If(@FifoTrolleyCard = '' Or @FifoTrolleyCard =  NULL)
				Begin
					SELECT 'Y' As Result,ModelNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,(OkQty - (ReOilingNgQty + FinalPackQty + QANgQty)) As Qty
					FROM Machining where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And (OkQty - (ReOilingNgQty + FinalPackQty + QANgQty)) > 0
				End
				Else
				Begin
					Select 'As per FIFO you have to scan '+ @FifoTrolleyCard + ' trolley card' As Result
				End
			End
		End
		Else If(@CardStatus = 2)
		Begin
			Select 'Final Packing already done' As Result
		End
		Else
		Begin
			Select 'Invalid status' As Result
		End
	End
	Else
	Begin
		Select 'Invalid Trolley No '+@TrolleyNo As Result
	End
END



GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_Get_FinalPacking_Data_Old] 
@TrolleyCard nvarchar(50) = null

AS
BEGIN
	Declare @FifoTrolleyCard varchar(50) = ''
	Declare @CardStatus int = 0,@Qty int,@ModelNo varchar(50),@MachineDate date,@ReOilingDate date = NULL

	Select @CardStatus = Status,@Qty = Sum(OkQty),@ModelNo = ModelNo,@ReOilingDate = Cast(ReOilingDate As Date) 
	,@MachineDate = Cast(PrintOn As Date) From Machining 
	Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And Status = 1 Group By Status,ModelNo,Cast(ReOilingDate As Date),Cast(PrintOn As Date)
	If(@CardStatus = 0)
	Begin
		Select 'Wrong Trolley Card Or Packing alredy done' As Result
		return
	End
	If(@CardStatus = 1)
	Begin
		-- If reoiling pending then need to check reoiling due date 
		If(@ReOilingDate IS NULL)
		Begin
			Declare @MonthInterVal int
			--Get Month Interval
			Select @MonthInterVal = Month_InterVal From ReOiling_Month
			--If Today date is after or on Reoiling date then return data
			Declare @DueDate date = DATEADD(M,@MonthInterVal,@MachineDate)
			--If trolley is due for reoiling
			if(Cast(GETDATE() As Date) >= @DueDate)
			Begin
				Select 'Trolley is due for reoiling, Machining date is ' + Convert(varchar,@MachineDate,103) + ' and reoiling date is '+ Convert(varchar,@DueDate,103) As Result
			End
			Else
			Begin
				SELECT Top(1) @FifoTrolleyCard = TrolleyCard FROM Machining Where LotNoDate <
				(
					SELECT Top(1) LotNoDate FROM Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard  Order By LotNoDate
				) And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status = 1
				 Order By LotNoDate
				If(@FifoTrolleyCard = '' Or @FifoTrolleyCard =  NULL)
				Begin
					SELECT DISTINCT 'Y' As Result,ModelNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,(OkQty - (ReOilingNgQty + FinalPackQty)) As Qty
					FROM Machining where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And (OkQty - (ReOilingNgQty + FinalPackQty)) > 0
				End
				Else
				Begin
					Select 'As per FIFO you have to scan '+ @FifoTrolleyCard + ' trolley card' As Result
				End
			End
		End
		Else -- if reoiling done then check other condition
		Begin
			--If Scanned trolley card is valid then check FIFO
			
			SELECT Top(1) @FifoTrolleyCard = TrolleyCard FROM Machining Where LotNoDate <
			(
				SELECT Top(1) LotNoDate FROM Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard  Order By LotNoDate
			) And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status = 1
			Order By LotNoDate
			If(@FifoTrolleyCard = '' Or @FifoTrolleyCard =  NULL)
			Begin
				SELECT 'Y' As Result,ModelNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,(OkQty - (ReOilingNgQty + FinalPackQty)) As Qty
				FROM Machining where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And (OkQty - (ReOilingNgQty + FinalPackQty)) > 0
			End
			Else
			Begin
				Select 'As per FIFO you have to scan '+ @FifoTrolleyCard + ' trolley card' As Result
			End
		End
	End
	Else If(@CardStatus = 2)
	Begin
		Select 'Final Packing already done' As Result
	End
	Else
	Begin
		Select 'Invalid status' As Result
	End

END



GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_Get_Machining_Data] 
@TrolleyCard nvarchar(50) = null

AS
BEGIN
	--Details should not return for One Particular model no
	Select ModelNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,(OkQty - (QASampleQty + QAPartialNgQty)) As TotalQty,Status From Cutting
	Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And ModelNo != 'HSPP-Z4M/Z4V' And (OkQty - (QASampleQty + QAPartialNgQty)) > 0
	Order By LotNoDate
		
END



GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON

GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_Get_Machining_Split_Data] 
@TrolleyCard nvarchar(50) = null

AS
BEGIN
	Declare @MachiningStatus int
	Select @MachiningStatus = Status From StatusMaster Where TableName='Cutting' 
	And EnumStatusValue = 'After_Machining';
	With CTE As
	(
		SELECT LotNo,(Sum(OkQty) + Sum(NgQty)) As MaQty FROM Machining 
		WHERE CuttingTrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard Group By LotNo
	)
	Select Cu.ModelNo,Cu.LotNo,Cu.LotNoDate,((Cu.OkQty - (QASampleQty + QAPartialNgQty)) - ISNULL(Ct.MaQty,0)) As TotalQty,
	Cu.Status 
	From CTE Ct Right Join Cutting Cu On Ct.LotNo = Cu.LotNo
	Where Cu.TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And Status != @MachiningStatus
		
END



GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_Get_ReOiling_Data] 
@TrolleyCard nvarchar(150) = null

AS
BEGIN
	
	Declare @CardStatus int = 0,@MachineDate date
	Select @CardStatus = Status,@MachineDate = Cast(PrintOn As Date) From Machining 
	Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And ReOilingDate Is Null 
	If(@CardStatus = 0)
	Begin
		Select 'Wrong Trolley Card Or ReOiling already done' As Result
	End
	Else If(@CardStatus = 1)
	Begin
		Declare @MonthInterVal int
		--Get Month Interval
		Select @MonthInterVal = Month_InterVal From ReOiling_Month
		--If Today date is after or on Reoiling date then return data
		Declare @DueDate date = DATEADD(M,@MonthInterVal,@MachineDate)
		if(Cast(GETDATE() As Date) >= @DueDate)
		Begin
			Select 'Y' As Result,ModelNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,(OkQty - QANgQty) As Qty From Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
		End
		Else
		Begin
			Select 'Trolley is not due for reoiling, Machining date is ' + Convert(varchar,@MachineDate,103) + ' and reoiling date is '+ Convert(varchar,@DueDate,103) As Result
		End
	End
	Else If(@CardStatus = 2)
	Begin
		Select 'Packing is already done for trolley card' As Result
	End
	Else
	Begin
		Select 'Invalid status' As Result
	End
		
END



GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_GetChargePalletNo]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetChargePalletNo]
(
	@ModelNo varchar(50),@LotNoDate varchar(50),@Line_No varchar(50)
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Declare @ChargeNo int,@PalletNo int
	--Get ChargeNo
	SELECT @ChargeNo = IsNull(Max(ChargeNo),0)
	FROM Cutting Where ModelNo = @ModelNo And LotNoDate = @LotNoDate And Line_No = @Line_No

	SELECT @PalletNo = IsNull(Max(PalletNo),0) 
	FROM Cutting Where ModelNo = @ModelNo And LotNoDate = @LotNoDate And ChargeNo = @ChargeNo And Line_No = @Line_No
	--Return Both Values
	Select @ChargeNo As ChargeNo,@PalletNo As PalletNo

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_GetCurrentShiftTrolleyCount]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetCurrentShiftTrolleyCount]
(@ShiftName varchar(50))
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--Get Trolley Count In Current Shift
	Declare @CuttingCount int = 0,@MachiningCount int = 0, @FinalPackCount int = 0
	Declare @DispatchCount int = 0,@ReceivingPendingCount int = 0 
	Select @ReceivingPendingCount = Count(TrolleyNo) From TrolleyMaster Where Status = 1
	If(@ShiftName = 'C')
	Begin
		Declare @CurrentTime time = GetDate()
		Declare @ShiftCEndTime time
		Select @ShiftCEndTime = EndTime from shiftmaster Where ShiftName='C'
		If(@CurrentTime <= @ShiftCEndTime) --Then Today And yesterday date will be included
		Begin
			--Get Cutting Trolley Count In Current Shift
			Select @CuttingCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyCard) From Cutting 
			Where (Cast(PrintOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) Or Cast(PrintOn As Date) = Cast(DateAdd(d,-1,GetDate()) As Date)) 
			And [Shift] = @ShiftName
			--Machining Count
			Select @MachiningCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyCard) From Machining 
			Where (Cast(PrintOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) Or Cast(PrintOn As Date) = Cast(DateAdd(d,-1,GetDate()) As Date)) 
			And [Shift] = @ShiftName
			--Final Pack Count
			Select @FinalPackCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyNo) From FinalPacking
			Where (Cast(PackOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) Or Cast(PackOn As Date) = Cast(DateAdd(d,-1,GetDate()) As Date))  
			And [Shift] = @ShiftName
			--Dispatch Count
			Select @DispatchCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyNo) From DispatchDetail
			Where (Cast(DispatchOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) Or Cast(DispatchOn As Date) = Cast(DateAdd(d,-1,GetDate()) As Date))  
			And [Shift] = @ShiftName
			--Return All Values
			Select IsNull(@CuttingCount,0) As CuttingCount,ISNull(@MachiningCount,0) As MachiningCount
			,IsNull(@FinalPackCount,0) As FinalPackCount,IsNull(@DispatchCount,0) As DispatchCount,@ReceivingPendingCount As ReceivingPendingCount
		End
		Else
		Begin
			--Get Cutting Trolley Count In Current Shift
			Select @CuttingCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyCard) From Cutting 
			Where Cast(PrintOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) And [Shift] = @ShiftName
			--Machining Count
			Select @MachiningCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyCard) From Machining 
			Where Cast(PrintOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) And [Shift] = @ShiftName
			--Final Pack Count
			Select @FinalPackCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyNo) From FinalPacking
			Where Cast(PackOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) And [Shift] = @ShiftName
			--Dispatch Count
			Select @DispatchCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyNo) From DispatchDetail
			Where Cast(DispatchOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) And [Shift] = @ShiftName
			--Return All Values
			Select IsNull(@CuttingCount,0) As CuttingCount,ISNull(@MachiningCount,0) As MachiningCount
			,IsNull(@FinalPackCount,0) As FinalPackCount,IsNull(@DispatchCount,0) As DispatchCount,@ReceivingPendingCount As ReceivingPendingCount
		End
	End
	Else
	Begin
		--Get Cutting Trolley Count In Current Shift
		Select @CuttingCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyCard) From Cutting 
		Where Cast(PrintOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) And [Shift] = @ShiftName
		--Machining Count
		Select @MachiningCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyCard) From Machining 
		Where Cast(PrintOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) And [Shift] = @ShiftName
		--Final Pack Count
		Select @FinalPackCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyNo) From FinalPacking
		Where Cast(PackOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) And [Shift] = @ShiftName
		--Dispatch Count
		Select @DispatchCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyNo) From DispatchDetail
		Where Cast(DispatchOn As Date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date) And [Shift] = @ShiftName
		--Return All Values
		Select IsNull(@CuttingCount,0) As CuttingCount,ISNull(@MachiningCount,0) As MachiningCount
		,IsNull(@FinalPackCount,0) As FinalPackCount,IsNull(@DispatchCount,0) As DispatchCount,@ReceivingPendingCount As ReceivingPendingCount
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_GetCustomer]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetCustomer]
(@Filter varchar(2),@CustomerName varchar(50)=NULL)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--Get All Customer Data
	If(@Filter = '1')
	Begin
		Select Id,CustomerName,[Location],(CustomerName + '-'+Location) As Customer From CustomerMaster Order By CustomerName,[Location]
	End
	--Get Only Customer Name
	Else If(@Filter = '2')
	Begin
		Select Distinct CustomerName From CustomerMaster Order By CustomerName
	End
	--Get Only Customer location based on Name
	Else If(@Filter = '3')
	Begin
		Select Distinct [Location] From CustomerMaster Where CustomerName = @CustomerName Order By [Location]
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_GetCuttingData]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetCuttingData]
(
	@GroupName varchar(50)=null,@LineNo varchar(50) = null,@IsPreviousMonth bit = 0,
	@PreviousMonth varchar(50) = null
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--Get Operator
	SELECT (UserId + '-' + UserName) As UserDetail,UserName FROM UserMaster Where GroupName = @GroupName ORDER BY UserName
	--Get Shift
	Exec [dbo].[Prc_GetShift]
	--Get Current Model No As Per Production Order And Pending Qty 
	--If fetching data for current month
	If(@IsPreviousMonth = 'False')
	Begin
		SELECT Top(1) ModelNo,Qty As PPQty,(Qty - ProducedQty) As PendingQty,ProductionPlanId FROM ProductionPlan 
		Where Month = Right(Replace(CONVERT(varchar,GETDATE(),106),' ','-'),8) And Line_No = @LineNo And Qty > ProducedQty
		Order BY OrderNo
	End
	Else --fetching data for previoius month
	Begin
		SELECT Top(1) ModelNo,Qty As PPQty,(Qty - ProducedQty) As PendingQty,ProductionPlanId FROM ProductionPlan 
		Where Month = @PreviousMonth And Line_No = @LineNo And Qty > ProducedQty
		Order BY OrderNo
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_GetDashBoardData]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetDashBoardData]
(
	@DashBoardName varchar(50),@IsPreviousDay bit =  0,@ProductionFlag int = 1,
	@ModelNo varchar(50) = NULL,@ShowNotUsedTrolley bit =  0
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--Show Trolley Count On DashBoard(Today/Previous Day)
	If(@DashBoardName = 'TROLLEYCOUNT')
	Begin
		Declare @CuttingCount int = 0,@MachiningCount int = 0, @FinalPackCount int = 0, @DispatchCount int = 0
		--Get Cutting Trolley Count
		Select @CuttingCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyCard) From Cutting 
		Where Cast(PrintOn As Date) = (Case When @IsPreviousDay = 'False' then Cast(GetDate() As Date) Else Cast(DATEADD(d,-1,GetDate()) As Date) End)
		--Machining Count
		Select @MachiningCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyCard) From Machining 
		Where Cast(PrintOn As Date) = (Case When @IsPreviousDay = 'False' then Cast(GetDate() As Date) Else Cast(DATEADD(d,-1,GetDate()) As Date) End)
		--Final Pack Count
		Select @FinalPackCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyNo) From FinalPacking
		Where Cast(PackOn As Date) = (Case When @IsPreviousDay = 'False' then Cast(GetDate() As Date) Else Cast(DATEADD(d,-1,GetDate()) As Date) End)
		--Dispatch Count
		Select @DispatchCount = Count(Distinct TrolleyNo) From DispatchDetail
		Where Cast(DispatchOn As Date) = (Case When @IsPreviousDay = 'False' then Cast(GetDate() As Date) Else Cast(DATEADD(d,-1,GetDate()) As Date) End)
		--Return All Values
		Select IsNull(@CuttingCount,0) As CuttingCount,ISNull(@MachiningCount,0) As MachiningCount
		,IsNull(@FinalPackCount,0) As FinalPackCount,IsNull(@DispatchCount,0) As DispatchCount
	End
	--Show Production related Data
	Else If(@DashBoardName = 'PRODUCTION')
	Begin
		Declare @ProdQty int = 0, @PendingQty int = 0, @OkQty int = 0, @NgQty int = 0, @TotalQty int = 0,@NgPer decimal(3,2)
		--Curent Production Qty,ProducedQty
		SELECT @ProdQty = Sum(Qty),@PendingQty =(Sum(Qty)- Sum(ProducedQty)) FROM ProductionPlan 
		Where Month = Right(Replace(CONVERT(varchar,GETDATE(),106),' ','-'),8) 
		--Get NgPercentage
		Select @NgPer = NgPerValue From NgPercentageValue
		--Get Ok & Ng Qty based on criteria
		--It means complete month prodction plan ok & ng qty
		If(@ProductionFlag = 1)
		Begin
			Select @TotalQty = Sum(TotalQty),@OkQty = Sum(OkQty),@NgQty = Sum(NGQty) From Cutting Where ProductionPlanId In
			(SELECT ProductionPlanId FROM ProductionPlan Where Month = Right(Replace(CONVERT(varchar,GETDATE(),106),' ','-'),8) )
		End
		--It means today production ok & ng qty
		Else If(@ProductionFlag = 2)
		Begin
			Select @TotalQty = Sum(TotalQty),@OkQty = Sum(OkQty),@NgQty = Sum(NGQty) From Cutting 
			Where Cast(PrintOn As date) = Cast(GetDate() As Date)
		End
		--It means previous day production ok & ng qty
		Else If(@ProductionFlag = 3)
		Begin
			Select @TotalQty = Sum(TotalQty),@OkQty = Sum(OkQty),@NgQty = Sum(NGQty) From Cutting 
			Where Cast(PrintOn As date) = Cast(DATEADD(d,-1,GetDate()) As Date)
		End
		--Return All data
		Select IsNull(@ProdQty,0) As PPQty,IsNull(@PendingQty,0) As PendingQty,IsNull(@OkQty,0) As OkQty,IsNull(@NgQty,0) As NgQty,
		IsNull(@TotalQty,0) As TotalQty,IsNull(@NgPer,0) As NgPer
	End
	--Show Inventory
	Else If(@DashBoardName = 'INVENTORY')
	Begin
		Declare @CuttingInventory int = 0,@MachiningInventory int = 0, @FinalPackInventory int = 0
		--Get Cutting Trolley Count
		Select @CuttingInventory = (Sum(OkQty) - (Sum(QASampleQty)+Sum(QAPartialNgQty))) From Cutting 
		Where Status ! =7 And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo +'%' --Machining Status
		--Machining Count
		Select @MachiningInventory = (Sum(OkQty) - (Sum(ReOilingNgQty)+Sum(QANgQty))) From Machining 
		Where Status = 1 And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo +'%' 
		--FinalPacking
		Select @FinalPackInventory = Sum(OkQty) From FinalPacking 
		Where Status = 1 And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo +'%'
		--Return All Values
		Select IsNull(@CuttingInventory,0) As CuttingInventory,ISNull(@MachiningInventory,0) As MachiningInventory
		,IsNull(@FinalPackInventory,0) As FinalPackInventory
	End
	--Show RECEIVING_PENDING Trolley Count Along with Cutomer name
	Else If(@DashBoardName = 'RECEIVING_PENDING')
	Begin
		--When Showing receiving pending trolley count with counter details
		If(@ShowNotUsedTrolley = 'False')
		Begin
			--Select CM.CustomerName,CM.Location, Count(TrolleyCount) As TrolleyCount From
			--(
			--	Select  Distinct DispatchOrderId,Count( Distinct TrolleyNo) As TrolleyCount From DispatchDetail Where TrolleyNo In
			--	(Select TrolleyNo From TrolleyMaster Where Status = 1 And IsReturnAble = 'True')
			--	Group By DispatchOrderId
			--) DD Join DispatchOrder DO On DD.DispatchOrderId =  DO.Id Join CustomerMaster CM 
			--On DO.CustomerId = Cm.Id Group By Cm.CustomerName,Cm.Location

			--Get trolle along with dispatch order which are  not in receiving table then join
			--with customer table to get customer details
			Select CM.CustomerName,CM.Location, Count(TrolleyNo) As TrolleyCount From
			(
				--Join trolley with Returnable table with dispatch order and trolley no
				Select DD.TrolleyNo,DD.DispatchOrderId,Tr.TrolleyNo As TR_TrolleyNo,Tr.DispatchOrderId As TR_DisOrderId From
				(
					--Filter Returnable and  dispatched trolley no along with dispatch order no
					Select distinct TrolleyNo,DispatchOrderId From DispatchDetail 
					Where TrolleyNo in(Select TrolleyNo From TrolleyMaster where Status=1 and IsReturnAble='True' )
				) DD Left Join TrolleyReceiving TR On DD.TrolleyNo=Tr.TrolleyNo And DD.DispatchOrderId = TR.DispatchOrderId
			) DDFinal Join DispatchOrder DO On DDFinal.DispatchOrderId =  DO.Id Join CustomerMaster CM 
						On DO.CustomerId = Cm.Id 
			 Where TR_TrolleyNo is null 
			 Group By Cm.CustomerName,Cm.Location

		End
		Else
		Begin
			Select  TrolleyNo,Description,PackSize From TrolleyMaster Where TrolleyNo
			Not In (Select Distinct TrolleyNo From FinalPacking) Order By TrolleyNo
		End
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_GetDispatchAvailableQty]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetDispatchAvailableQty]
(@Filter varchar(2),@ModelNo varchar(50)=NULL)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--Get Only Totol Qty
	If(@Filter = '1')
	Begin
		Declare @OkQty int,@ReserQty int
		Select @OkQty = IsNull(Sum(OkQty),0)  From  FinalPacking Where ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status = 1
		Select @ReserQty = IsNull(Sum(ReservedQty),0)  From  DispatchReservedQty Pack Where ModelNo = @ModelNo
		Select (@OkQty - @ReserQty) As Qty
	End
	--Get trolley wise qty
	Else If(@Filter = '2')
	Begin
		Select TrolleyNo,(IsNull(Sum(OkQty),0) - IsNull(Sum(Dis.ReservedQty),0))  As Qty,Cast(PackOn as date) PackOn From  FinalPacking Pack Left Join DispatchReservedQty Dis
		On Pack.ModelNo = Dis.ModelNo Where Pack.ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status = 1
		Group By TrolleyNo,Cast(PackOn as date) Order By PackOn

	End
	
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_GetDispatchData]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetDispatchData]
(
	@Filter varchar(2),@DispatchOrderNo varchar(50)=null,@ModelNo varchar(50)=NULL
	,@DispatchOrderId numeric(18,0)=null,@TrolleyNo varchar(50)=null
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--Get Data Based on dispatch order no
	If(@Filter = '1')
	Begin
		SELECT D.Id, ModelNo,Qty,DispatchQty,CM.CustomerName,CM.Location FROM DispatchOrder D Join CustomerMaster CM On D.CustomerId = CM.Id
		Where DispatchOrderNo = @DispatchOrderNo
		And Qty > DispatchQty 
	End
	--Get Trolley Qty against model
	Else If(@Filter = '2')
	Begin
		If Exists(Select TrolleyNo From TrolleyMaster Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And Status = 1)
		Begin
			Select 'Trolley already dispatched' As Result
			return
		End
		Declare @Qty int = 0
		Select @Qty = IsNull(Sum(OkQty),0) From FinalPacking Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo 
		And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status = 1
		If(@Qty > 0)
		Begin
			--If trolley valid then check fifo
			Declare @FifoTrolleyNo varchar(50) = ''
			SELECT Top(1) @FifoTrolleyNo = TrolleyNo FROM FinalPacking Where Cast(PackOn as date) <
			(
				SELECT Top(1) Cast(PackOn as date) As PackOn FROM FinalPacking Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And Status = 1  Order By Cast(PackOn as date)
			) And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status = 1
			 Order By Cast(PackOn as date)
			If(@FifoTrolleyNo = '' Or @FifoTrolleyNo =  NULL)
			Begin
				Select 'Y' As Result,@Qty As Qty
			End
			Else
			Begin
				Select 'As per FIFO you have to scan '+ @FifoTrolleyNo + ' trolley no' As Result
			End
		End
		Else
		Begin
			Select 'Trolley details not found,possible reasons are # Trolley already dispatched # Wrong trolley no  #Available qty 0  # Model does not belong to trolley' As Result
		End
	End
END
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_GetRePrintData]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetRePrintData]
(
	@ReprintType varchar(50),@TrolleyCard varchar(50)
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	If(@ReprintType = 'CUTTING')
	Begin
		SELECT ModelNo,Sum(OkQty) - (Sum(QASampleQty) +  Sum(QAPartialNgQty)) As OkQty 
		FROM Cutting Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
		Group By ModelNo
	End
	Else If(@ReprintType = 'MACHINING')
	Begin
		SELECT ModelNo,Sum(OkQty) - (Sum(QANgQty) + Sum(ReOilingNgQty)) As OkQty 
		FROM Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
		Group By ModelNo
	End
END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetShift]
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	
	--Get Shift
	--  Select ShiftName,Convert(varchar(5),GetDate(),108),Cast(Convert(varchar(5),GetDate(),108) as time)  
	--From ShiftMaster Where Cast(Convert(varchar(5),GetDate(),108) as time)
	--between StartTime And EndTime

	 Declare @CurrentTime as time = getdate() 

	 Select ShiftName,@CurrentTime From ShiftMaster 
		Where StartTime <= @CurrentTime and @CurrentTime < EndTime
	   or EndTime < StartTime and @CurrentTime < EndTime 
	   or EndTime < StartTime and StartTime <= @CurrentTime 

END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_GetTimerTime_PendingReOiling]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetTimerTime_PendingReOiling]
(
	@Type Varchar(50) = NULL
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	If(@Type = 'Time')
	Begin
		Select * From TimerTimeSetting Order By Process
	End
	Else
	Begin
		Declare @MonthInterVal int
		--Get Month Interval
		Select @MonthInterVal = Month_InterVal From ReOiling_Month
		--Return Pending ReOiling Count
		Select Count(Distinct TrolleyCard) As Total From Machining
		Where Cast(GETDATE() As Date) >= DATEADD(M,@MonthInterVal,Cast(PrintOn As Date))
		And Status = 1 And ReOilingDate Is Null
	End

END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_GetTrolleyNo]
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--Get Trolley
    SELECT TrolleyNo,PackQty,PackSize FROM TrolleyMaster WHERE IsEmpty = 'TRUE' ORDER BY TrolleyNo

END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_GroupMaster]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_GroupMaster] 
@Type varchar(20),
@GroupName varchar(50)=null,
@ModuleId int=null,
@CreatedBy varchar(100)=null
as
  Begin
	if(@Type='SELECT')
	  begin
		Select GroupName,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn
			  from GroupMaster Order By GroupName
		Select ModuleId,ModuleName From ModuleMaster Where Active = 'True' Order By ModuleId
	  end
	else if(@Type='SELECTBYID')
	  begin
			Select ModuleId From GroupRight Where GroupName = @GroupName
	  end	  
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
	 
	    Insert Into GroupMaster (GroupName,CreatedBy,CreatedOn)
	    values(@GroupName,@CreatedBy,GETDATE())
	    
		Select 'SUCCESS'
		end
	  else if(@Type='INSERT_GROUP_RIGHT')
	  begin
	    INSERT INTO [dbo].[GroupRight]
           ([GroupName]
           ,[ModuleId]
           ,[CreatedOn]
           ,[CreatedBy]) VALUES(@GroupName,@ModuleId,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy)
		 Select 'SUCCESS'
	  end
	else if(@Type='DELETE_GROUP_RIGHT')
	  begin
	    Delete From GroupRight Where GroupName = @GroupName
		 Select 'SUCCESS'
	  end
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	  begin
		  Begin Try
			Begin Tran
				 delete from GroupMaster
				 WHERE GroupName=@GroupName

				 Delete From GroupRight Where GroupName = @GroupName

				 Select 'SUCCESS'
			Commit Tran
		End Try
		Begin Catch
			Rollback Tran
			Select 'DB Error-'+  ERROR_MESSAGE()
		End Catch
	  end
	
  End







GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_LineMaster]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_LineMaster] 
@Type varchar(max),
@LineNo nvarchar(50)=null,
@Description nvarchar(250)=null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50)=null

AS
BEGIN
	Declare @Count int;
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			SELECT Line_No,Description,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM LineMaster ORDER BY Line_No
		end
	else if (@Type = 'SEARCH')
		begin
			SELECT Line_No,Description,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM LineMaster
			WHERE Line_No like '%' + @LineNo + '%'
		end
	else if(@Type='SELECTBYID')
	  begin
		SELECT Line_No,Description,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM LineMaster
		WHERE Line_No = @LineNo
	  end
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
	    INSERT INTO [dbo].LineMaster
           (Line_No
           ,[Description]
           ,[CreatedOn]
           ,[CreatedBy])
		 VALUES
           (@LineNo
           ,@Description
           ,GETDATE()
           ,@CreatedBy)

			Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	 else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	  begin
	     UPDATE [dbo].LineMaster
		   SET Description = @Description
		 WHERE Line_No = @LineNo
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	  begin
	     delete from dbo.LineMaster WHERE Line_No = @LineNo
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end

END



GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_MachineMaster] 
@Type varchar(max),
@MachineNo nvarchar(50)=null,
@Description nvarchar(250)=null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50)=null

AS
BEGIN
	Declare @Count int;
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			SELECT MachineNo,Description,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM MachineMaster ORDER BY MachineNo
		end
	else if (@Type = 'SEARCH')
		begin
			SELECT MachineNo,Description,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM MachineMaster
			WHERE MachineNo like '%'+@MachineNo+'%'
		end
	else if(@Type='SELECTBYID')
	  begin
		SELECT MachineNo,Description,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM MachineMaster
		WHERE MachineNo = @MachineNo
	  end
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
	    INSERT INTO [dbo].[MachineMaster]
           ([MachineNo]
           ,[Description]
           ,[CreatedOn]
           ,[CreatedBy])
		 VALUES
           (@MachineNo
           ,@Description
           ,GETDATE()
           ,@CreatedBy)

			Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	 else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	  begin
	     UPDATE [dbo].[MachineMaster]
		   SET Description = @Description
		 WHERE MachineNo = @MachineNo
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	  begin
	     delete from dbo.[MachineMaster] WHERE MachineNo = @MachineNo
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end

END



GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_MachiningHold]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_MachiningHold] 
@Type varchar(max),
@TrolleyCard nvarchar(50) = null,
@HoldStatus bit = null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50) = null

AS
BEGIN
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			if Exists(Select TrolleyCard From Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard)
			Begin
				Select 'Y' As Result
			End
			Else
			Begin
				Select 'Invalid TrolleyCard '+@TrolleyCard As Result
			End
		end
	else if (@Type = 'UPDATE') -- update the status for trolley barcode
		begin
			if Exists(Select TrolleyCard From Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard)
			Begin
				Update Machining Set IsHold = @HoldStatus,HoldOn = GETDATE(),HoldBy = @CreatedBy
				Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
				Select 'Y' As Result
			End
			Else
			Begin
				Select 'Invalid TrolleyCard '+@TrolleyCard As Result
			End
		end
	
END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_ModelMaster]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_ModelMaster] 
@Type varchar(max),
@ModelNo nvarchar(50)=null,
@Description nvarchar(250)=null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50)=null,
@DTB int = null,
@CuttingMaxQty int = null
AS
BEGIN
	Declare @Count int;
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			SELECT ModelNo,Description,DTB,CuttingMaxQty,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM ModelMaster ORDER BY ModelNo
		end
	else if (@Type = 'SEARCH')
		begin
			SELECT ModelNo,DTB,Description,CuttingMaxQty,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM ModelMaster
			WHERE ModelNo like '%' + @ModelNo + '%'
		end
	else if(@Type='SELECTBYID')
	  begin
		SELECT ModelNo,DTB,Description,CuttingMaxQty,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM ModelMaster
		WHERE ModelNo = @ModelNo
	  end
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
	    INSERT INTO [dbo].ModelMaster
           (ModelNo
           ,[Description]
		   ,DTB
           ,[CreatedOn]
           ,[CreatedBy],CuttingMaxQty)
		 VALUES
           (@ModelNo
           ,@Description
		   ,@DTB
           ,GETDATE()
           ,@CreatedBy,@CuttingMaxQty)

			Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	 else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	  begin
	     UPDATE [dbo].ModelMaster
		   SET Description = @Description,DTB = @DTB,CuttingMaxQty = @CuttingMaxQty
		   ,ModifyOn = GetDate(),ModifyBy = @CreatedBy
		 WHERE ModelNo = @ModelNo
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	  begin
	     delete from dbo.ModelMaster WHERE ModelNo = @ModelNo
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end

END



GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_NGPercentage] 
@Type varchar(max),
@PercentageValue decimal(3,2)

AS
BEGIN
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			SELECT NgPerValue FROM NgPercentageValue
		end
	
	 else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	  begin
	     Update NgPercentageValue Set NgPerValue = @PercentageValue
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	

END

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Picking_For_Machining_Data]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_Picking_For_Machining_Data] 
@Type varchar(max),@TrolleyCard nvarchar(50) = null,@Status int=null,@UserId varchar(50)=null

AS
BEGIN
	If(@Type = 'SELECT')
	Begin
		Declare @CardStatus int = 0,@Qty int,@ModelNo varchar(50),@Line_No varchar(50)
		Select @CardStatus = Status,@Qty = (Sum(OkQty) - (Sum(QASampleQty)+Sum(QAPartialNgQty))),@ModelNo = ModelNo,@Line_No = Line_No From Cutting 
		Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard Group By Status,ModelNo,Line_No
		If(@CardStatus = 0)
		Begin
			Select 'Wrong Trolley Card' As Result
		End
		Else If(@CardStatus = 1)
		Begin
			Select 'QA pending' As Result
		End
		Else If(@CardStatus = 2)
		Begin
			--If Scanned trolley card is valid then check FIFO
			Declare @FifoTrolleyCard varchar(50) = ''
			SELECT Top(1) @FifoTrolleyCard = TrolleyCard FROM CUTTING Where LotNoDate <
			(
				SELECT Top(1) LotNoDate FROM CUTTING Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard  Order By LotNoDate
			) And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Status In (1,2) And (OkQty -QAPartialNgQty) > 0 --partial qty will be done after ok
			And Line_No= @Line_No Order By LotNoDate
			If(@FifoTrolleyCard = '' Or @FifoTrolleyCard =  NULL)
			Begin
				Select 'Y' As Result,@Qty As Qty,@ModelNo As ModelNo
			End
			Else
			Begin
				Select 'As per FIFO you have to scan '+ @FifoTrolleyCard + ' trolley card' As Result
			End
		End
		Else If(@CardStatus = 3)
		Begin
			Select 'QA Ng for trolley' As Result
		End
		Else If(@CardStatus = 4)
		Begin
			Select 'Trolley is on hold' As Result
		End
		Else If(@CardStatus = 5)
		Begin
			Select 'QA is not defined after sampling' As Result
		End
		Else If(@CardStatus = 6)
		Begin
			Select 'Picking already done' As Result
		End
		Else If(@CardStatus = 7)
		Begin
			Select 'Machining already done' As Result
		End
		Else
		Begin
			Select 'Invalid status' As Result
		End
		
	End
	Else If(@Type = 'UPDATE')
	Begin
		Update Cutting Set Status = @Status,PickOn = GetDate(),PickBy = @UserId Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
		Select 'Y' As Result,'Picking Complete' As Msg
	End
END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_ProductionPlan]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_ProductionPlan] 
@Type varchar(max),
@Month nvarchar(50) = null,
@MonthNo int = null,
@Year int = null,
@OrderNo int = null,
@ModelNo nvarchar(50) = null,
@Qty int = null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50) = null,@Remarks varchar(500) = null,@LineNo varchar(50) = null

AS
BEGIN
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			SELECT ProductionPlanId,Line_No,Month,OrderNo,ModelNo,Qty,ProducedQty,Remarks,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn 
			,ModifiedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),ModifiedOn,103) ModifiedOn 
			FROM ProductionPlan --Where Qty > ProducedQty 
			--ORDER BY Year,MonthNo,OrderNo
			ORDER BY Year Desc,MonthNo Desc,Line_No,OrderNo
		end
	else if (@Type = 'SEARCH')
		begin
			SELECT ProductionPlanId,Line_No,Month,OrderNo,ModelNo,Qty,ProducedQty,Remarks,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn 
			,ModifiedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),ModifiedOn,103) ModifiedOn 
			FROM ProductionPlan Where Month Like '%' + @Month + '%' 
			--And Qty > ProducedQty 
			ORDER BY Year Desc,MonthNo Desc,Line_No,OrderNo
		end
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
		--Check whether order no assigned to some other model
		Declare @Model varchar(50) = ''
		Select @Model = @ModelNo From ProductionPlan Where Month = @Month And OrderNo = @OrderNo And Line_No = @LineNo
		--If order no not assigned to any model then save
		If(@Model = '')
		Begin
			INSERT INTO [dbo].[ProductionPlan]
           ([Month]
           ,[MonthNo]
           ,[Year]
           ,[OrderNo]
           ,[ModelNo]
           ,[Qty]
           ,[ProducedQty]
           ,[CreatedOn]
           ,[CreatedBy],Line_No
           )
		 VALUES
			   (@Month
			   ,@MonthNo
			   ,@Year
			   ,@OrderNo
			   ,@ModelNo
			   ,@Qty
			   ,0
			   ,GETDATE()
			   ,@CreatedBy,@LineNo
			   )

				Select 'Y' AS RESULT
		End
		Else
		Begin
			Select 'Order no is already assigned to Model No ' + @Model AS RESULT
		End
	  end
	 else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	  begin
		Begin Try
			Begin Tran
				--If qty is decreasing then it can not be lesser than produced qty
				Declare @ProdQty int,@ProductionPlanId numeric(18,0)
				Select @ProdQty = ProducedQty,@ProductionPlanId = ProductionPlanId From ProductionPlan Where Month = @Month And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Line_No = @LineNo
				if(@Qty >= @ProdQty)
				Begin
					--While updating if order no is updating then order no will be interchange some other model who
					-- has same order no
					--Get Old order No
					Declare @Order int
					Select @Order = OrderNo From ProductionPlan Where Month = @Month And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Line_No = @LineNo
					--Update Model who has new order no
					Update ProductionPlan Set OrderNo = @Order Where Month = @Month And Line_No = @LineNo And OrderNo = @OrderNo
					--Update new Order No
					 UPDATE [dbo].ProductionPlan
					   SET Qty = @Qty,
					 OrderNo = @OrderNo,ModifiedBy = @CreatedBy,
					 ModifiedOn = GETDATE(),Remarks = @Remarks
					  WHERE Month = @Month And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Line_No = @LineNo
					  --Store history of production  plan change
					  Insert Into ProductionPlan_ChangeHistory(ProductionPlanId,Remarks,ChangeBy,ChangeOn)
					  Values(@ProductionPlanId,@Remarks,@CreatedBy,GETDATE())
					 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
				 End
				 Else
				 Begin
					Select 'Production already started, qty can not be lesser than '+ cast(@ProdQty as varchar) AS RESULT
				 End
			 Commit Tran
		End Try
		Begin Catch
			Rollback Tran
			Select 'DB Error-'+  ERROR_MESSAGE() As RESULT
		End Catch
	  end
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	  begin
		--Delete only if no production started
		If not exists(Select ModelNo from dbo.ProductionPlan WHERE Month = @Month And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Line_No = @LineNo And ProducedQty > 0)
		Begin
			 Delete from dbo.ProductionPlan WHERE Month = @Month And ModelNo = @ModelNo And Line_No = @LineNo
			 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
		End
		Else
		Begin
			Select 'Could not delete,production already started' AS RESULT
		End
	  end
END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_QA]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_QA] 
@Type varchar(max),
@TrolleyCard nvarchar(50) = null,
@Status int = null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50) = null,
@Shift nvarchar(50) = null,
@PartialNgQty int = null,
@NgReason varchar(500)=null,
@LotNo varchar(50) = null
AS
BEGIN
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			Select Status,LotNo+' # '+Cast(OkQty - (QASampleQty + QAPartialNgQty) As varchar) As LotNo
			From Cutting Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
		end
	else if (@Type = 'UPDATE') -- update the status for trolley barcode
		begin
			--In case of hold status update hold on date to track when it was on hold
			UPDATE Cutting SET Status = @Status,QAOn = GETDATE(),QABy =@CreatedBy,QAShift = @Shift
			Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
			--If Hold Status Date Separtely
			If(@Status = 4)
			Begin
				UPDATE Cutting SET QAHoldOn = GETDATE() 
				Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
			End
			--If partial ng
			If(@PartialNgQty > 0)
			Begin
				Update Cutting Set QAPartialNgQty = QAPartialNgQty + @PartialNgQty,QAPartialNgReason = @NgReason 
				Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And LotNo = @LotNo
			End
			
			Select 'Y' As Result
		end
	
END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_QA_Machining]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_QA_Machining] 
@Type varchar(max),
@TrolleyCard nvarchar(50) = null,
@IsHold bit = null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50) = null,
@QANgQty int = null,
@NgReason varchar(500) = null,
@LotNo varchar(50) = null
AS
BEGIN
	If (@Type = 'SELECT')
	Begin
		Select Status,LotNo+' # '+Cast(OkQty - (ReOilingNgQty + QANgQty) As varchar) As LotNo
		From Machining Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
	End
	Else If (@Type = 'UPDATE') -- update the status for trolley barcode
	Begin
		-- If Hold Then Update Hold Status
		If(@IsHold = 'True')
		Begin
			UPDATE Machining SET IsHold = 'True',HoldBy=@CreatedBy, HoldOn = GETDATE() 
			Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
		End
		Else --Update Partial NG Qty
		Begin
			Update Machining Set QANgQty = QANgQty + @QANgQty,QaNgReason = @NgReason,QAOn = GetDate() 
			,QABy = @CreatedBy,IsHold = 'False' Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And LotNo = @LotNo
		End
			
		Select 'Y' As Result
	End
	
END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_QASample]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_QASample] 
@Type varchar(max),
@TrolleyCard nvarchar(50) = null,
@Status int = null,
@PickedQty int = null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50) = null

AS
BEGIN
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			Declare @CardStatus int = 0,@Qty int
			Select @CardStatus = Status,@Qty = (Sum(OkQty) - (Sum(QASampleQty)+Sum(QAPartialNgQty))) From Cutting Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard
			Group By Status
			If(@CardStatus = 0)
			Begin
				Select 'Wrong Trolley Card' As Result
			End
			Else If(@CardStatus <= 5)
			Begin
				Select 'Y' As Result,@Qty As Qty
			End
			Else
			Begin
				Select 'Invalid status' As Result
			End
		end
	else if (@Type = 'UPDATE') -- update the status for trolley barcode
		begin
			--loop the all rows against trolley card and adjust qty as per ok qty
			Declare @OkQty int,@Id numeric(18,0)
			While Exists(Select TrolleyCard From Cutting Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard And OkQty > (QASampleQty+QAPartialNgQty))
			Begin
				Select Top(1) @OkQty = (OkQty - (QASampleQty+QAPartialNgQty)),@Id =Id From Cutting Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard 
				And OkQty > (QASampleQty+QAPartialNgQty) Order By Id
			
				If(@OkQty > @PickedQty)
				Begin
					Update Cutting Set QASampleQty = QASampleQty + @PickedQty,QASampleOn = GETDATE(),QASampleBy = @CreatedBy  Where Id = @Id
					break
				End
				Else
				Begin
					Update Cutting Set QASampleQty = QASampleQty + @OkQty,QASampleOn = GETDATE(),QASampleBy = @CreatedBy  Where Id = @Id
					Set @PickedQty = @PickedQty - @OkQty
				End
			End

			Select 'Y' As Result
		end
	
END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_Cutting]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_Cutting]
(
	@FromDate datetime,@ToDate datetime,@ModelNo varchar(50),@LotNo varchar(50),@Id numeric(18,0),
	@ReportType varchar(10),@LineNo varchar(10)
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--When showing without ng report
	If(@ReportType = '1')
	Begin
		Select Id,Line_No,ModelNo,Shift,LotNo,Operator,Leader,TotalQty,OkQty,NGQty,
		TrolleyCard,(Case When Status = 1 Then 'Yes' Else 'No' End) QAPending,CONVERT(varchar(10),PrintOn,103) As PrintOn From Cutting 
		Where Cast(PrintOn As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(PrintOn As Date) <= @ToDate
		And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' And LotNo Like '%' + @LotNo + '%' And Line_No Like '%' + @LineNo + '%'
		Order By PrintOn
	End
	--When showing NG report
	else If(@ReportType = '2')
	Begin
		SELECT [InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[PenetrationPorosity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],[ForeignSubstance],[Crack]
		,[MaterialLD],[OD],[Cutting],[Other],[DTB],[Sample],[PowerCut],[Length],[ExtraParam5]
		FROM [dbo].[CuttingDefect] Where CuttingId = @Id
	End
	--When showing combine report with ng details
	else If(@ReportType = '3')
	Begin
		Select ModelNo,Line_No,Shift,LotNo,Operator,Leader,TotalQty,OkQty,NGQty,
		TrolleyCard,(Case When Status = 1 Then 'Yes' Else 'No' End) QAPending,CONVERT(varchar(10),PrintOn,103) As PrintOn 
		,[InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[PenetrationPorosity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],[ForeignSubstance],[Crack]
		,[MaterialLD],[OD],[Cutting],[Other],[DTB],[Sample],[PowerCut],[Length],[ExtraParam5]
		From Cutting Left Join CuttingDefect On Cutting.Id =  CuttingDefect.CuttingId
		Where Cast(PrintOn As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(PrintOn As Date) <= @ToDate
		And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' And LotNo Like '%' + @LotNo + '%' And Line_No Like '%' + @LineNo + '%'
		Order By PrintOn
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_Dispatch]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_Dispatch]
(
	@FromDate datetime,@ToDate datetime,@ModelNo varchar(50)=null
	,@CustomerId numeric(18,0)=null,@TrolleyNo varchar(50)=null
)
AS
BEGIN
	
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

		Select DO.Id As DispatchOrderId,CONVERT(varchar,DD.DispatchOn,100) As DispatchDate,
		(Cm.CustomerName+'-'+CM.Location) As Customer,DD.ModelNo,DD.TrolleyNo,Sum(DD.Qty) As DispatchQty
		 ,(Case When Isnull(Tr.Status,0) = 0 Then 'No' Else 'Yes' End) As IsTrolleyReceived
		 From DispatchOrder DO Join DispatchDetail DD On DO.Id = DD.DispatchOrderId
		 Join CustomerMaster CM On Do.CustomerId = CM.Id Left Join TrolleyReceiving Tr
		 On DD.DispatchOrderId = Tr.DispatchOrderId And DD.TrolleyNo = Tr.TrolleyNo
		 Where DO.DispatchDate >= @FromDate And DO.DispatchDate  <= @ToDate And 
		 DO.ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' And DD.TrolleyNo = (Case When @TrolleyNo = '' Then DD.TrolleyNo Else @TrolleyNo End) 
		And Do.CustomerId = (Case When @CustomerId = 0 Then DO.CustomerId Else @CustomerId End) 
		 Group By Do.Id,CONVERT(varchar,DD.DispatchOn,100),(Cm.CustomerName+'-'+CM.Location),DD.ModelNo,DD.TrolleyNo,Tr.Status
	
	Order By DispatchDate,Customer,ModelNo

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_FinalPacking]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_FinalPacking]
(
	@FromDate datetime,@ToDate datetime,@ModelNo varchar(50),@LotNo varchar(50),@Id numeric(18,0),
	@ReportType varchar(10)
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	

	--When showing without ng report
	If(@ReportType = '1')
	Begin
		Select Distinct Ma.Line_No As [LineNo], Fp.Id,Fp.[Shift],FP.ModelNo,Fp.LotNo,Fp.TotalQty,Fp.OkQty,Fp.NGQty,
		FP.TrolleyNo,(Case When Tm.IsEmpty = 1 then 'Yes' Else 'No' End) As IsEmpty,CONVERT(varchar(10),PackOn,103) As PackOn,
		PackBy,Fp.[Status],Ma.Operator As MachiningOperator,Ma.Inspector As MachiningInspector,CONVERT(varchar(10),Ma.PrintOn,103) As MachiningOn
		From FinalPacking FP Join TrolleyMaster TM On Fp.TrolleyNo = Tm.TrolleyNo 
		Join Machining Ma On Fp.MachiningTrolleyCard =  Ma.TrolleyCard
		Where Cast(PackOn As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(PackOn As Date) <= @ToDate
		And Fp.ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' And Fp.LotNo Like '%' + @LotNo + '%'
		Order By PackOn,TrolleyNo
	End
	--When showing NG report
	else If(@ReportType = '2')
	Begin
		SELECT [InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],PackingNg,[Other]
      ,Rust,ExtraParam2,ExtraParam3,[ExtraParam4],[ExtraParam5] FROM [dbo].FinalPackingDefect Where FinalPackingId = @Id
	End
	--When showing combine report with ng details
	else If(@ReportType = '3')
	Begin
		Select Distinct Ma.Line_No As [LineNo],Fp.[Shift],Fp.ModelNo,Fp.LotNo,Fp.TotalQty,Fp.OkQty,Fp.NGQty,Fp.TrolleyNo,(Case When Tm.IsEmpty = 1 then 'Yes' Else 'No' End) As IsEmpty,
		CONVERT(varchar(10),PackOn,103) As PackOn,PackBy,Fp.[Status],Ma.Operator As MachiningOperator,Ma.Inspector As MachiningInspector,CONVERT(varchar(10),Ma.PrintOn,103) As MachiningOn
		,[InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],PackingNg,[Other]
		,Rust,ExtraParam2,ExtraParam3,[ExtraParam4],[ExtraParam5]
		From FinalPacking FP Join TrolleyMaster TM On Fp.TrolleyNo = Tm.TrolleyNo 
		Left Join FinalPackingDefect On FP.Id = FinalPackingDefect.FinalPackingId
		Join Machining Ma On Fp.MachiningTrolleyCard =  Ma.TrolleyCard
		Where Cast(PackOn As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(PackOn As Date) <= @ToDate
		And Fp.ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' And Fp.LotNo Like '%' + @LotNo + '%'
		Order By PackOn,TrolleyNo
	End

END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_Inventory]
(
	@ModelNo varchar(50) = null
)
AS
BEGIN
	-- If trolley goes for machining it means QA OK
	SET NOCOUNT ON;

	Select ModelNo,Sum(OkQty) As Qty From FinalPacking Where ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo +'%' 
	And Status = 1 Group By ModelNo
	Order By ModelNo

END
GO

SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_Machining]
(
	@FromDate datetime,@ToDate datetime,@ModelNo varchar(50),@LotNo varchar(50),@Id numeric(18,0),
	@ReportType varchar(10),@LineNo varchar(50)
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	

	--When showing without ng report
	If(@ReportType = '1')
	Begin
		Select Id,[Shift],ModelNo,Line_No As [LineNo],LotNo,TotalQty,OkQty,NGQty,TrolleyCard,CONVERT(varchar(10),PrintOn,103) As PrintOn
		,PrintBy,Operator,Inspector From Machining 
		Where Cast(PrintOn As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(PrintOn As Date) <= @ToDate
		And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' And LotNo Like '%' + @LotNo + '%'
		And Line_No Like '%' + @LineNo + '%'
		Order By PrintOn
	End
	--When showing NG report
	else If(@ReportType = '2')
	Begin
		SELECT [InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],[MCNg],[Other]
      ,[ID-],[ID+],[PowerCut],[ExtraParam4],[ExtraParam5] FROM [dbo].MachiningDefect Where MachiningId = @Id
	End
	--When showing combine report with ng details
	else If(@ReportType = '3')
	Begin
		Select [Shift],ModelNo,Line_No As [LineNo],LotNo,TotalQty,OkQty,NGQty,TrolleyCard,CONVERT(varchar(10),PrintOn,103) As PrintOn,
		PrintBy,Operator,Inspector,[InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],[MCNg],[Other]
      ,[ID-],[ID+],[PowerCut],[ExtraParam4],[ExtraParam5]
		From Machining Left Join MachiningDefect On Machining.Id = MachiningDefect.MachiningId
		Where Cast(PrintOn As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(PrintOn As Date) <= @ToDate
		And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' And LotNo Like '%' + @LotNo + '%'
		And Line_No Like '%' + @LineNo + '%'
		Order By PrintOn
	End

END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_Picking]
(
	@FromDate datetime,@ToDate datetime,@ModelNo varchar(50),@LotNo varchar(50),@Id numeric(18,0),
	@ReportType varchar(10)
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--When showing without ng report
	If(@ReportType = '1')
	Begin
		Select Id,ModelNo,LotNo,TotalQty,OkQty,NGQty,
		TrolleyCard,CONVERT(varchar(10),PickOn,103) As PickOn,PickBy From Cutting 
		Where PickOn Is Not Null And Cast(PickOn As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(PickOn As Date) <= @ToDate
		And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' And LotNo Like '%' + @LotNo + '%'
		Order By PickOn
	End
	--When showing NG report
	else If(@ReportType = '2')
	Begin
		SELECT [InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[PenetrationPorosity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],[ForeignSubstance],[Crack]
		,[MaterialLD],[OD],[Cutting],[Other],[DTB],[Sample],[PowerCut],[Length],[ExtraParam5]
		FROM [dbo].[CuttingDefect] Where CuttingId = @Id
	End
	--When showing combine report with ng details
	else If(@ReportType = '3')
	Begin
		Select ModelNo,LotNo,TotalQty,OkQty,NGQty,
		TrolleyCard,CONVERT(varchar(10),PickOn,103) As PickOn,PickBy 
		,[InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[PenetrationPorosity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],[ForeignSubstance],[Crack]
		,[MaterialLD],[OD],[Cutting],[Other],[DTB],[Sample],[PowerCut],[Length],[ExtraParam5]
		From Cutting Left Join CuttingDefect On Cutting.Id =  CuttingDefect.CuttingId
		Where PickOn Is Not Null And Cast(PickOn As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(PickOn As Date) <= @ToDate
		And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' And LotNo Like '%' + @LotNo + '%'
		Order By PickOn
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_QA]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_QA]
(
	@FromDate datetime,@ToDate datetime,@ModelNo varchar(50),@LotNo varchar(50),@LineNo varchar(50)
)
AS
BEGIN
	-- If trolley goes for machining it means QA OK
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Select ModelNo,LotNo,QABy,Line_No,
	(Case When Status = 2 Or Status = 6 Or Status = 7 then 'OK' When Status = 3 Then 'NG' Else 'HOLD' End) As Status,
	TrolleyCard,CONVERT(varchar(10),QAOn,103) As QAOn From Cutting 
	Where Cast(QAOn As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(QAOn As Date) <= @ToDate
	And Status In (2,3,4,6,7) 
	And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' And LotNo Like '%' + @LotNo + '%'
	And Line_No Like '%' + @LineNo + '%'
	Order By QAOn,TrolleyCard

END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_ReOiling]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_ReOiling]
(
	@FromDate datetime,@ToDate datetime,@ModelNo varchar(50),@IsPending bit
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--If Showing Pending For ReOiling
	If(@IsPending = 'True')
	Begin
		Declare @MonthInterVal int
		--Get Month Interval
		Select @MonthInterVal = Month_InterVal From ReOiling_Month
		--Return Pending ReOiling Count
		Select ModelNo,TrolleyCard,SUM(TotalQty) As TotalQty,SUM(OkQty) As OkQty,SUM(NgQty) As NgQty
		,CONVERT(varchar,PrintOn,103) As ProcessDate,PrintBy As UserName From Machining
		Where Cast(GETDATE() As Date) >= DATEADD(M,@MonthInterVal,Cast(PrintOn As Date))
		And Status = 1 And ReOilingDate Is Null
		Group By ModelNo,TrolleyCard,CONVERT(varchar,PrintOn,103),PrintBy
	End
	Else	--When Showing Completed reoiling data
	Begin
		Select ModelNo,MachiningTrolleyCard As TrolleyCard,SUM(TotalQty) As TotalQty,SUM(OkQty) As OkQty
		,SUM(NgQty) As NgQty,CONVERT(varchar,ReOilingDate,103) As ProcessDate,ReOilingBy As UserName From ReOiling
		Where Cast(ReOilingDate As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(ReOilingDate As Date) <= @ToDate
		And ModelNo Like '%' + @ModelNo + '%' 
		Group By ModelNo,MachiningTrolleyCard,CONVERT(varchar,ReOilingDate,103),ReOilingBy
		Order By ProcessDate
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_TrolleyReceiving]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Rpt_TrolleyReceiving]
(
	@Type varchar(50),@FromDate datetime,@ToDate datetime,@TrolleyNo varchar(50)
	,@CustomerId numeric(18,0)=null,@TrayQty int=null,@ColorName varchar(50),@Id numeric(18,0)=null
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--It will return trolley no to be used as filter
	If(@Type = '1')
	Begin
		Select TrolleyNo From TrolleyMaster Order By CreatedOn
	End
	Else If(@Type = '2') -- return all data for trolley receiving
	Begin
		Select Tr.Id,(Cm.CustomerName+'-'+CM.Location) As Customer,TrolleyNo,TryQty As TrayQty,
		ColorName,CONVERT(varchar,Tr.CreatedOn,100) As CreatedOn
		,Tr.CreatedBy From TrolleyReceiving Tr Join DispatchOrder Do On Tr.DispatchOrderId = Do.Id
		Join CustomerMaster CM On Do.CustomerId = CM.Id
		Where Cast(Tr.CreatedOn As Date) >= @FromDate And Cast(Tr.CreatedOn As Date) <= @ToDate
		And Tr.TrolleyNo Like '%' + @TrolleyNo + '%' And Do.CustomerId = (Case When @CustomerId = 0 Then DO.CustomerId Else @CustomerId End) 
		Order By Tr.CreatedOn
	End
	Else -- Update details
	Begin
		Update TrolleyReceiving Set TryQty = @TrayQty,ColorName= @ColorName
		Where Id= @Id
	End
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_SaveCuttingData]
(
	@ProdPlanId numeric(18,0),@ModelNo varchar(50),@Shift varchar(50),@ChargeNo int = NULL,@PalletNo int = NULL,@LineNo varchar(50)=NULL,@LotNo varchar(50),@LotNoDate varchar(50),
	@Operator varchar(250),@Leader varchar(250),@TotalQty int,@OkQty int,@NgQty int,@TrolleyCard varchar(50),
	@Status int,@CreatedBy varchar(50),@InnerCavity int = NULL,@OuterCavity int = NULL,
	@PenetrationPorosity int = NULL,@Slag int = NULL,@Dent int = NULL,@Spine int = NULL,
	@ForeignSubstance int = NULL,@Crack int = NULL,@MaterialLD int = NULL,@OD int = NULL,
	@Cutting int = NULL,@Other int = NULL,@DTB int = NULL,@Sample int = NULL,
	@PowerCut int = NULL,@Length int = NULL,@ExtraParam5 int = NULL
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Begin Try
		Begin Tran
			If(@LineNo = '' Or @LineNo Is Null)
			Begin
				Set @LineNo = SUBSTRING(@LotNo,7,1)
			End
			--Insert data in Cutting Table 
			INSERT INTO [dbo].[Cutting]
           ([ProductionPlanId] ,[ModelNo] ,[Shift],ChargeNo,PalletNo,Line_No ,[LotNo],LotNoDate,[Operator],[Leader]
           ,[TotalQty],[OkQty],[NGQty],[TrolleyCard],[Status],[PrintOn],[PrintBy] )
			VALUES
           (@ProdPlanId,@ModelNo,@Shift,@ChargeNo,@PalletNo,@LineNo,@LotNo,@LotNoDate,@Operator,@Leader,@TotalQty,@OkQty
           ,@NgQty,@TrolleyCard,@Status,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy)

		   Declare @CuttingId numeric(18,0)
		   --It will return inserted id(Identity column value)
		   Set @CuttingId = @@IDENTITY
		   --Insert Defect if ng qty
		   If(@NgQty > 0)
		   Begin
				INSERT INTO [dbo].[CuttingDefect]
			   (
				   [CuttingId],[InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[PenetrationPorosity],[Slag],[Dent]
				   ,[Spine],[ForeignSubstance],[Crack],[MaterialLD],[OD],[Cutting],[Other]
				   ,DTB,[Sample],PowerCut,[Length],[ExtraParam5],[CreatedOn],[CreatedBy]
			   )
				 VALUES
					   (@CuttingId,@InnerCavity,@OuterCavity,@PenetrationPorosity,@Slag,@Dent,@Spine
					   ,@ForeignSubstance,@Crack,@MaterialLD,@OD,@Cutting,@Other,@DTB,@Sample
					   ,@PowerCut,@Length,@ExtraParam5,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy)
		   End
		   
		   --Update Produced Qty
		   Update ProductionPlan Set ProducedQty = ProducedQty + @OkQty Where ProductionPlanId = @ProdPlanId
		  
		Commit Tran
		 Select 'Y' As Result
	End Try
	Begin Catch
		RollBack Tran
		DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000);  
		DECLARE @ErrorSeverity INT;  
		DECLARE @ErrorState INT;  
  
		SELECT   
		@ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),  
		@ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),  
		@ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();  
   
		RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, -- Message text.  
			@ErrorSeverity, -- Severity.  
			@ErrorState -- State.  
			);
		--Select 'DB Error-' + ERROR_MESSAGE() As Result
	End Catch
END
GO
