CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_SaveDispatchData]
(
	@DispatchOrderId numeric(18,0),@Shift varchar(50),@ModelNo varchar(50),@TrolleyNo varchar(50),
    @FinalPackStatus int, @TrolleyStatus int,@Qty int,@CreatedBy varchar(50)
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Begin Try
	
		Begin Tran
			--Insert data in dispatch details table# data will come from final packing table
			INSERT INTO [dbo].[DispatchDetail]([DispatchOrderId],[Shift],[ModelNo],[TrolleyNo]
			,[LotNo],[LotNoDate],[MachiningTrolleyCard],[Qty],[DispatchOn],[DispatchBy])
			Select @DispatchOrderId,@Shift,ModelNo,@TrolleyNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,MachiningTrolleyCard,OkQty,
			GETDATE(),@CreatedBy From FinalPacking Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And Status = 1
			--Update Dispatch order qty
			Update DispatchOrder Set DispatchQty = DispatchQty + @Qty Where Id = @DispatchOrderId
			--Remove reserve qty as it has dispatch now 
			Update DispatchReservedQty Set ReservedQty = ReservedQty - @Qty Where ModelNo = @ModelNo
			--Update Trolley status in final packing
			Update FinalPacking Set Status = @FinalPackStatus Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
			--Update TrolleyStatus
			Update TrolleyMaster Set Status = @TrolleyStatus Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
		Commit Tran
		Select 'Y' As Result
	End Try
	Begin Catch
		RollBack Tran
		DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000);  
		DECLARE @ErrorSeverity INT;  
		DECLARE @ErrorState INT;  
  
		SELECT   
		@ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),  
		@ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),  
		@ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();  
   
		RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, -- Message text.  
			@ErrorSeverity, -- Severity.  
			@ErrorState -- State.  
			);
		--Select 'DB Error-' + ERROR_MESSAGE() As Result
	End Catch
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_SaveFinalPackingData]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_SaveFinalPackingData]
(
	@Shift varchar(50),@ModelNo varchar(50),@TrolleyNo varchar(50),@TrolleyPackSize int,@LotNo varchar(50),@LotNoDate varchar(50),@MachiningTrolleyCard varchar(50),
    @FinalPackStatus int,@MachiningStatus int,@TotalQty int,@OkQty int,@NgQty int,@CreatedBy varchar(50),@InnerCavity int = NULL,@OuterCavity int = NULL,
	@Slag int = NULL,@Dent int = NULL,@Spine int = NULL,
	@PackNg int = NULL,@Other int = NULL,@Rust int = NULL,@ExtraParam2 int = NULL,
	@ExtraParam3 int = NULL,@ExtraParam4 int = NULL,@ExtraParam5 int = NULL
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Begin Try
	
		Begin Tran
			--Insert data in FinalPacking Table 
			INSERT INTO [dbo].[FinalPacking]
           ([Shift],[ModelNo],[TrolleyNo],[LotNo],[LotNoDate],[MachiningTrolleyCard],[Status]
           ,[TotalQty],[OkQty],[NgQty],[PackOn],[PackBy])
			VALUES(@Shift,@ModelNo,@TrolleyNo,@LotNo,@LotNoDate,@MachiningTrolleyCard
			,@FinalPackStatus,@TotalQty,@OkQty,@NgQty,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy)

		   Declare @FinalPackId numeric(18,0)
		   --It will return inserted id(Identity column value)
		   Set @FinalPackId = @@IDENTITY
		   --Insert Defect if ng qty
		   If(@NgQty > 0)
		   Begin
				INSERT INTO [dbo].[FinalPackingDefect]
			   ([FinalPackingId],[InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],[PackingNg]
			   ,[Other],[Rust],[ExtraParam2],[ExtraParam3],[ExtraParam4],[ExtraParam5],[CreatedOn],[CreatedBy])
				VALUES
				(@FinalPackId,@InnerCavity,@OuterCavity,@Slag,@Dent,@Spine,@PackNg,@Other
				,@Rust,@ExtraParam2,@ExtraParam3,@ExtraParam4,@ExtraParam5,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy)
		   End
			--Update Machining
		   Update Machining Set FinalPackQty = FinalPackQty + (@OkQty + @NgQty) Where TrolleyCard = @MachiningTrolleyCard
		   And ModelNo = @ModelNo And LotNo = @LotNo 
		   --Update Machining
		   Update Machining Set Status = @MachiningStatus Where TrolleyCard = @MachiningTrolleyCard
		   And ModelNo = @ModelNo And LotNo = @LotNo And @TotalQty = (@OkQty + @NgQty)
		  --Update TrolleyPackSize if user has change it manually
		  --Update Only if pack size has changed
		  If Exists(Select TrolleyNo From TrolleyMaster Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And PackSize != @TrolleyPackSize)
		  Begin
				Update TrolleyMaster Set PackSize = @TrolleyPackSize,ModifyOn = GETDATE(),ModifyBy = @CreatedBy
				Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
		  End
		  --Updat Trolley
		  Update TrolleyMaster Set PackQty = PackQty + @OkQty Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
		  --Update Trolley Status
		  Update TrolleyMaster Set IsEmpty = 'False' Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo And PackSize =  PackQty
		Commit Tran
		 Select 'Y' As Result
	End Try
	Begin Catch
		RollBack Tran
		DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000);  
		DECLARE @ErrorSeverity INT;  
		DECLARE @ErrorState INT;  
  
		SELECT   
		@ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),  
		@ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),  
		@ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();  
   
		RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, -- Message text.  
			@ErrorSeverity, -- Severity.  
			@ErrorState -- State.  
			);
		--Select 'DB Error-' + ERROR_MESSAGE() As Result
	End Catch
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_SaveMachiningData]
(
	@Shift varchar(50),@ModelNo varchar(50),@LotNo varchar(50),@LotNoDate varchar(50),@LineNo varchar(50),@CuttingTrolleyCard varchar(50),
    @TotalQty int,@OkQty int,@NgQty int,@TrolleyCard varchar(50),
	@Status int,@MachiningStatus int,@CreatedBy varchar(50),@OperatorName varchar(50),@InspectorName varchar(50),
	@InnerCavity int = NULL,@OuterCavity int = NULL,@Slag int = NULL,@Dent int = NULL,@Spine int = NULL,
	@McNg int = NULL,@Other int = NULL,@IDPlus int = NULL,@IDMinus int = NULL,
	@PowerCut int = NULL,@ExtraParam4 int = NULL,@ExtraParam5 int = NULL
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Begin Try
	
		Begin Tran
			--Insert Cutting Trolley Card Line No into Maching Table
			Declare @CuttingLineNo varchar(50)
			Set @CuttingLineNo = SUBSTRING(@LotNo,7,1)
			--Insert data in Machining Table 
			INSERT INTO [dbo].[Machining]
           ([Shift],ModelNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,[Line_No],[CuttingTrolleyCard],[TotalQty],[OkQty],[NgQty],[TrolleyCard]
           ,[Status],[PrintOn],[PrintBy],Operator,Inspector,CuttingLineNo)
			VALUES
           (@Shift,@ModelNo,@LotNo,@LotNoDate,@LineNo,@CuttingTrolleyCard,@TotalQty,@OkQty,@NgQty,@TrolleyCard
           ,@MachiningStatus,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy,@OperatorName,@InspectorName,@CuttingLineNo)

		   Declare @MachiningId numeric(18,0)
		   --It will return inserted id(Identity column value)
		   Set @MachiningId = @@IDENTITY
		   --Insert Defect if ng qty
		   If(@NgQty > 0)
		   Begin
				INSERT INTO [dbo].[MachiningDefect]
			   ([MachiningId],[InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],[MCNg]
			   ,[Other],[ID+],[ID-],PowerCut,[ExtraParam4],[ExtraParam5]
			   ,[CreatedOn],[CreatedBy])
				VALUES
			   (@MachiningId,@InnerCavity,@OuterCavity,@Slag,@Dent,@Spine,@McNg,@Other,@IDPlus
			   ,@IDMinus,@PowerCut,@ExtraParam4,@ExtraParam5,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy)
		   End
		
		   --Update Cutting
		   Update Cutting Set Status = @Status Where TrolleyCard = @CuttingTrolleyCard
		  --After Save Remove Maching Temp Table Data
		  --Exec [Prc_Machining_Temp] 'DELETE'
		Commit Tran
		 Select 'Y' As Result
	End Try
	Begin Catch
		RollBack Tran
		DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000);  
		DECLARE @ErrorSeverity INT;  
		DECLARE @ErrorState INT;  
  
		SELECT   
		@ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),  
		@ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),  
		@ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();  
   
		RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, -- Message text.  
			@ErrorSeverity, -- Severity.  
			@ErrorState -- State.  
			);
		--Select 'DB Error-' + ERROR_MESSAGE() As Result
	End Catch
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_SaveMachiningSplitData]
(
	@Shift varchar(50),@ModelNo varchar(50),@LotNo varchar(50),@LotNoDate varchar(50),@LineNo varchar(50),@CuttingTrolleyCard varchar(50),
    @TotalQty int,@OkQty int,@NgQty int,@TrolleyCard varchar(50),
	@Status int,@MachiningStatus int,@CreatedBy varchar(50),@OperatorName varchar(50),@InspectorName varchar(50),
	@InnerCavity int = NULL,@OuterCavity int = NULL,@Slag int = NULL,@Dent int = NULL,@Spine int = NULL,
	@McNg int = NULL,@Other int = NULL,@IDPlus int = NULL,@IDMinus int = NULL,
	@PowerCut int = NULL,@ExtraParam4 int = NULL,@ExtraParam5 int = NULL
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	--Check Same Lot With Same Model Is  exist
	If Exists(Select TrolleyCard From Machining Where ModelNo = @ModelNo And LotNo = @LotNo)
	Begin
		DECLARE @ErrorState2 INT;
		SELECT @ErrorState2 = ERROR_STATE();
		RAISERROR ('Same LotNo with same model already exist!!',16, 1);
		return
	End
	Begin Try
		Begin Tran
			--Insert Cutting Trolley Card Line No into Maching Table
			Declare @CuttingLineNo varchar(50)
			Set @CuttingLineNo = SUBSTRING(@LotNo,7,1)
			--Insert data in Machining Table 
			INSERT INTO [dbo].[Machining]
			([Shift],ModelNo,LotNo,LotNoDate,[Line_No],[CuttingTrolleyCard],[TotalQty],[OkQty],[NgQty],[TrolleyCard]
			,[Status],[PrintOn],[PrintBy],Operator,Inspector,CuttingLineNo)
			VALUES
			(@Shift,@ModelNo,@LotNo,@LotNoDate,@LineNo,@CuttingTrolleyCard,@TotalQty,@OkQty,@NgQty,@TrolleyCard
			,@MachiningStatus,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy,@OperatorName,@InspectorName,@CuttingLineNo)

			Declare @MachiningId numeric(18,0)
			--It will return inserted id(Identity column value)
			Set @MachiningId = @@IDENTITY
			--Insert Defect if ng qty
			If(@NgQty > 0)
			Begin
				INSERT INTO [dbo].[MachiningDefect]
				([MachiningId],[InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],[MCNg]
				,[Other],[ID+],[ID-],PowerCut,[ExtraParam4],[ExtraParam5]
				,[CreatedOn],[CreatedBy])
				VALUES
				(@MachiningId,@InnerCavity,@OuterCavity,@Slag,@Dent,@Spine,@McNg,@Other,@IDPlus
				,@IDMinus,@PowerCut,@ExtraParam4,@ExtraParam5,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy)
			End
		
			--Update Cutting
			Declare @CuttingTotalQty int,@MachiningTotalQty int
			Select @CuttingTotalQty = (Sum(OkQty) - (Sum(QASampleQty) + Sum(QAPartialNgQty))) From Cutting Where TrolleyCard = @CuttingTrolleyCard
			Select @MachiningTotalQty = (Sum(OkQty) + Sum(NgQty)) From Machining Where CuttingTrolleyCard = @CuttingTrolleyCard
			If(@CuttingTotalQty = @MachiningTotalQty)
			Begin
				Update Cutting Set Status = @Status Where TrolleyCard = @CuttingTrolleyCard
			End
			Commit Tran
			Select 'Y' As Result
	
	End Try
	Begin Catch
		RollBack Tran
		DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000);  
		DECLARE @ErrorSeverity INT;  
		DECLARE @ErrorState INT;  
  
		SELECT   
		@ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),  
		@ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),  
		@ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();  
   
		RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, -- Message text.  
			@ErrorSeverity, -- Severity.  
			@ErrorState -- State.  
			);
		--Select 'DB Error-' + ERROR_MESSAGE() As Result
	End Catch
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_SaveReOilingData]
(
	@Shift varchar(50),@ModelNo varchar(50),@LotNo varchar(50),@LotNoDate varchar(50),@MachiningTrolleyCard varchar(50),
    @TotalQty int,@OkQty int,@NgQty int,@CreatedBy varchar(50),@InnerCavity int = NULL,@OuterCavity int = NULL,
	@Slag int = NULL,@Dent int = NULL,@Spine int = NULL,
	@RoNg int = NULL,@Other int = NULL,@ExtraParam1 int = NULL,@ExtraParam2 int = NULL,
	@ExtraParam3 int = NULL,@ExtraParam4 int = NULL,@ExtraParam5 int = NULL
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	Begin Try
	
		Begin Tran
			--Insert data in ReOiling Table 
			INSERT INTO [dbo].[ReOiling]
           ([Shift],[ModelNo],LotNo,LotNoDate,[MachiningTrolleyCard],[TotalQty],[OkQty],[NgQty],[ReOilingDate],[ReOilingBy])
			 VALUES
           (@Shift,@ModelNo,@LotNo,@LotNoDate,@MachiningTrolleyCard,@TotalQty,@OkQty,@NgQty,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy)

		   Declare @ReOilingId numeric(18,0)
		   --It will return inserted id(Identity column value)
		   Set @ReOilingId = @@IDENTITY
		   --Insert Defect if ng qty
		   If(@NgQty > 0)
		   Begin
				INSERT INTO [dbo].[ReOilingDefect]
			   (ReOilingId,[InnerCavity],[OuterCavity],[Slag],[Dent],[Spine],[RoNg]
			   ,[Other],[ExtraParam1],[ExtraParam2],[ExtraParam3],[ExtraParam4],[ExtraParam5]
			   ,[CreatedOn],[CreatedBy])
				VALUES
			   (@ReOilingId,@InnerCavity,@OuterCavity,@Slag,@Dent,@Spine,@RoNg,@Other,@ExtraParam1
			   ,@ExtraParam2,@ExtraParam3,@ExtraParam4,@ExtraParam5,GETDATE(),@CreatedBy)
		   End
		
		   --Update Machining
		   Update Machining Set ReOilingNgQty = @NgQty,ReOilingDate = GETDATE(),ReOilingBy = @CreatedBy Where 
		   TrolleyCard = @MachiningTrolleyCard And ModelNo = @ModelNo And LotNo = @LotNo
		  
		Commit Tran
		 Select 'Y' As Result
	End Try
	Begin Catch
		RollBack Tran
		DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000);  
		DECLARE @ErrorSeverity INT;  
		DECLARE @ErrorState INT;  
  
		SELECT   
		@ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),  
		@ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),  
		@ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();  
   
		RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, -- Message text.  
			@ErrorSeverity, -- Severity.  
			@ErrorState -- State.  
			);
		--Select 'DB Error-' + ERROR_MESSAGE() As Result
	End Catch
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_ShiftMaster]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_ShiftMaster] 
@Type varchar(max),
@ShiftName nvarchar(50)=null,
@StartTime nvarchar(50)=null,
@EndTime nvarchar(50)=null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50)=null

AS
BEGIN
	Declare @Count int;
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			SELECT ShiftName,CONVERT(VARCHAR(5),StartTime,108) As StartTime,CONVERT(VARCHAR(5),EndTime,108) As EndTime,
			CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM ShiftMaster ORDER BY StartTime
		end
	else if (@Type = 'SEARCH')
		begin
			SELECT ShiftName,CONVERT(VARCHAR(5),StartTime,108) As StartTime,CONVERT(VARCHAR(5),EndTime,108) As EndTime,
			CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM ShiftMaster
			WHERE ShiftName like '%' + @ShiftName + '%'
		end
	else if(@Type='SELECTBYID')
	  begin
		SELECT ShiftName,CONVERT(VARCHAR(5),StartTime,108) As StartTime,CONVERT(VARCHAR(5),EndTime,108) As EndTime,
			CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM ShiftMaster
		WHERE ShiftName = @ShiftName
	  end
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
		--Start Time Should Be Greater than last inserted end time
		Declare @LastEndTime time(7) = ''
		Select Top(1) @LastEndTime = EndTime From ShiftMaster Order By EndTime Desc
		if(@StartTime >= @LastEndTime)
		Begin
			INSERT INTO [dbo].ShiftMaster
			   (ShiftName
			   ,StartTime
			   ,EndTime
			   ,[CreatedOn]
			   ,[CreatedBy])
			 VALUES
			   (@ShiftName
			   ,@StartTime
			   ,@EndTime
			   ,GETDATE()
			   ,@CreatedBy)

				Select 'Y' AS RESULT
		End
		Else
			Select 'Start Time should be greater than ' + CONVERT(VARCHAR(5),@LastEndTime,108)  AS RESULT
	  end
	 --else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	 -- begin
	 --    UPDATE [dbo].ShiftMaster
		--   SET Description = @Description
		-- WHERE ModelNo = @ModelNo
		-- Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	 -- end
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	  begin
	     delete from dbo.ShiftMaster WHERE ShiftName = @ShiftName
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	  else if(@Type='SHIFT')
	  begin
	     Select *,Convert(varchar(5),GetDate(),108),Cast(Convert(varchar(5),GetDate(),108) as time)  
		From ShiftMaster Where Cast(Convert(varchar(5),GetDate(),108) as time)
		 between StartTime And EndTime
	  end
END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[PRC_TROLLEY_REC]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:24 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROC [dbo].[PRC_TROLLEY_REC]
@TYPE NVARCHAR(50),
@TROLLEY NVARCHAR(100)=NULL,
@TRY_QTY DECIMAL(18,0)=NULL,
@COLOR NVARCHAR(50)=NULL,
@CREATED_BY NVARCHAR(50)=NULL
AS
BEGIN
  IF @TYPE='GET_COLOR'
   BEGIN
       SELECT ColorName FROM ColorMaster Order By ColorName
   END
   IF @TYPE='VALID_TROLLEY'
   BEGIN
   
			IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT TrolleyNo FROM TrolleyMaster WHERE TrolleyNo=@TROLLEY)
			  BEGIN
	     			Select 'Invalid Trolley' AS RESULT
					RETURN;
			  END
		ELSE IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT TrolleyNo FROM TrolleyMaster WHERE TrolleyNo=@TROLLEY and Status=1)
		BEGIN
	     	Select 'Trolley Not Dispatched' AS RESULT
			RETURN;
		END
		ELSE
		     BEGIN
	    			Select 'OK' AS RESULT
					RETURN;
			  END 
   END
  IF @TYPE='SAVE_TROLLEY_REC'
   BEGIN
			IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT TrolleyNo FROM TrolleyMaster WHERE TrolleyNo=@TROLLEY)
			  BEGIN
	     			Select 'Invalid Trolley' AS RESULT
					RETURN;
			  END
			IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT TrolleyNo FROM TrolleyMaster WHERE TrolleyNo=@TROLLEY and Status=1)
			  BEGIN
	     			Select 'Trolley Not Dispatched' AS RESULT
					RETURN;
			  END
			
  
			BEGIN TRAN
				 BEGIN TRY
						--Get Dispatch Order For Trolley
						Declare @DispatchOrderId numeric(18,0)
						Select Top(1) @DispatchOrderId =  DispatchOrderId From DispatchDetail 
						Where TrolleyNo = @TROLLEY Order By DispatchOn Desc
						INSERT INTO [dbo].[TrolleyReceiving]
								   (DispatchOrderId,[TrolleyNo]
								   ,[TryQty]
								   ,[ColorName]
								   ,[Status]
								   ,[CreatedBy]
								   ,[CreatedOn])
						VALUES
								   (@DispatchOrderId,@TROLLEY
								   ,@TRY_QTY
								   ,@COLOR
								   ,1
								   ,@CREATED_BY
								   ,GETDATE())

					 UPDATE TrolleyMaster SET Status=0,IsEmpty=1,PackQty=0 WHERE TrolleyNo=@TROLLEY AND Status=1
				
			COMMIT TRAN
						 Select 'Y' As Result,'Saved Successfully'
						END TRY
					 BEGIN CATCH
						  IF @@TRANCOUNT>0
							 BEGIN
							   ROLLBACK
							 END
							SELECT 
							ERROR_MESSAGE() AS ErrorMessage,ERROR_LINE() as line;
					 END CATCH
  END

   
END

GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_TrolleyMaster]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:25 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_TrolleyMaster] 
@Type varchar(max),
@TrolleyNo nvarchar(50)=null,
@Description nvarchar(250)=null,
@IsReturnAble bit=null,
@PackSize int=null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50)=null

AS
BEGIN
	Declare @Count int;
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			SELECT TrolleyNo,Description,PackSize,IsReturnAble,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM TrolleyMaster ORDER BY TrolleyNo
		end
	else if (@Type = 'SEARCH')
		begin
			SELECT TrolleyNo,Description,PackSize,IsReturnAble,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM TrolleyMaster
			WHERE TrolleyNo like '%' +@TrolleyNo + '%'
		end
	else if(@Type='SELECTBYID')
	  begin
		SELECT TrolleyNo,Description,PackSize,IsReturnAble,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM TrolleyMaster
		WHERE TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
	  end
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
	    INSERT INTO [dbo].TrolleyMaster
           (TrolleyNo
           ,[Description],
		   PackSize
           ,[CreatedOn]
           ,[CreatedBy],IsReturnAble)
		 VALUES
           (@TrolleyNo
           ,@Description
		   ,@PackSize
           ,GETDATE()
           ,@CreatedBy,@IsReturnAble)

			Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	 else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	  begin
	     UPDATE [dbo].TrolleyMaster
		   SET Description = @Description,
		   PackSize = @PackSize,ModifyOn = GetDate(),ModifyBy=@CreatedBy,IsReturnAble = @IsReturnAble
		 WHERE TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	  begin
	     delete from dbo.TrolleyMaster WHERE TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_TrolleyMaster_FromHHT]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:25 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_TrolleyMaster_FromHHT] 
@Type varchar(max),
@TrolleyNo nvarchar(50)=null,
@ModelNo nvarchar(50)=null,
@PackSize int=null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50)=null

AS
BEGIN
	 if (@Type = 'SEARCH')
		begin
			SELECT TrolleyNo,PackSize,ModelNo
			FROM TrolleyMaster Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo
		end
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
		If Exists(Select TrolleyNo From TrolleyMaster Where TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo)
		Begin
			Select 'Trolley No already exist' AS RESULT
		End
		Else
		Begin
			INSERT INTO [dbo].TrolleyMaster
			   (TrolleyNo,
			   [Description]
			   ,ModelNo,
			   PackSize
			   ,[CreatedOn]
			   ,[CreatedBy])
			 VALUES
			   (@TrolleyNo
			   ,@TrolleyNo
			   ,@ModelNo
			   ,@PackSize
			   ,GETDATE()
			   ,@CreatedBy)

				Select 'Y' AS RESULT
			End
	  end

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_Update_Cutting_Trolley]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:25 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_Update_Cutting_Trolley]
(
	@Type varchar(max),@Id numeric(18,0)=NULL,@LotNo varchar(50),@LotNoDate varchar(50),@TrolleyCard varchar(50),
	@UserId varchar(50) = NULL,@IsValueChange bit = 'False',@OldTrolleyCard varchar(50) = NULL
	,@NewModelNo varchar(50) = '',@UpdateType int = 1,@TotalQty int = 0,@OkQty int = 0, @NgQty int = 0
)
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	If(@Type = 'SELECT')
	Begin
		Select Id,Status,LotNo As ChargePallet,TotalQty,OkQty,NgQty From Cutting Where TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard Order By Id
	End
	else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	Begin
		--When lot is being updated
		If(@UpdateType = 1)
		Begin
			If(@IsValueChange = 'True')
			Begin
				Declare @ModelNo varchar(50)
				Select @ModelNo =  ModelNo From Cutting Where TrolleyCard = @OldTrolleyCard
				If Not Exists(Select LotNo From Cutting Where LotNo = @LotNo And ModelNo = @ModelNo)
				Begin
					--Insert Log
					Declare @OldLotNo varchar(50),@LineNo varchar(50)
					Select @OldLotNo = LotNo From Cutting Where Id = @Id
					INSERT INTO [dbo].[Cutting_Trolley_Update_Log]
					   ([Cutting_Id],[Old_LotNo],[New_LotNo] ,[Old_TrolleyCard],[New_TrolleyCard],[UpdateOn],[UpdateBy])
					 VALUES
					   (@Id,@OldLotNo,@LotNo,@OldTrolleyCard,@TrolleyCard,GETDATE(),@UserId)
					--Update New Trolley Lot No
					Set @LineNo = SUBSTRING(@LotNo,7,1)
					Update Cutting Set LotNo = @LotNo,LotNoDate = @LotNoDate,ChargeNo=SUBSTRING(@LotNo,8,2),PalletNo=right(@LotNo,2),Line_No = @LineNo Where Id = @Id
					--Update New Trolley Trolley card
					Update Cutting Set TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard Where TrolleyCard = @OldTrolleyCard
					Select 'Y' As Result
				End
				Else
				Begin
					SELECT 'Lot No '+ @LotNo + ' already exist' As Result
				End
			End
			Else
				Select 'Y' As Result
		End
		Else If(@UpdateType = 2)-- When model is being update
		Begin
			Update Cutting Set ModelNo = @NewModelNo,TrolleyCard = @TrolleyCard Where TrolleyCard = @OldTrolleyCard
			Select 'Y' As Result
		End
		Else -- @UpdateType = 3 Qty update
		Begin
			Update Cutting Set TotalQty = @TotalQty,OkQty = @OkQty, NgQty = @NgQty Where TrolleyCard = @OldTrolleyCard
			Select 'Y' As Result
		End
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_UserMaster]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:25 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[Prc_UserMaster] 
@Type varchar(max),
@UserID nvarchar(50)=null,
@UserName nvarchar(150)=null,
@Password nvarchar(50)=null,
@Group nvarchar(50)=null,
@CreatedBy nvarchar(50)=null,
@NewPassword nvarchar(50)=null

AS
BEGIN
	Declare @Count int;
	if (@Type = 'SELECT')
		begin
			SELECT USERID,USERNAME,PASSWORD,GROUPNAME,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM UserMaster ORDER BY USERNAME
		end
	else if (@Type = 'SEARCH')
		begin
			SELECT USERID,USERNAME,PASSWORD,GROUPNAME,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM UserMaster 
			WHERE USERID like '%'+@UserID+'%'
		end
	else if(@Type='SELECTBYID')
	  begin
		SELECT USERID,USERNAME,PASSWORD,GROUPNAME,CreatedBy,CONVERT(varchar(10),CreatedOn,103) CreatedOn FROM UserMaster 
			WHERE USERID = @UserID
	  end
	else if(@Type='INSERT')
	  begin
	    INSERT INTO [dbo].[UserMaster]
           ([UserId]
           ,[UserName]
           ,[Password]
           ,[GroupName]
           ,[CreatedOn]
           ,[CreatedBy])
		 VALUES
           (@UserID
           ,@UserName
           ,@Password
           ,@Group
           ,GETDATE()
           ,@CreatedBy)

			Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	 else if(@Type='UPDATE')
	  begin
	     UPDATE [dbo].[UserMaster]
		   SET [UserName] = @UserName
			  ,[Password] = @Password
			  ,[GroupName] = @Group
		 WHERE UserId = @UserId
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	else if(@Type='DELETE')
	  begin
	     delete from dbo.[UserMaster] WHERE UserId=@UserID
		 Select 'Y' AS RESULT
	  end
	
	else if (@Type='VALIDATEUSER') 
		    begin
			      Select UserName,GroupName,USERID From UserMaster Where UserId = @UserID And Password = @Password
		    end
	else if (@Type='UPDATEPASSWORD')
		begin
			Declare @UserOldPassword varchar(50)
			Select @UserOldPassword = Password From UserMaster Where UserId = @UserID
			If(@Password = @UserOldPassword)
			Begin
				UPDATE UserMaster set PASSWORD = @NewPassword where  UserId=@UserID
				Select 'Y' AS RESULT
			End
			Else
			Begin
				Select 'Wrong Old Password' AS RESULT
			End
		end

END



GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[Prc_ValidateTrolleyNo]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:25 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[Prc_ValidateTrolleyNo]
(@TrolleyNo varchar(50))
AS
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	
	Declare @PackQty int,@PackSize int = 0,@IsEmpty bit
    SELECT @PackQty = PackQty,@PackSize = PackSize,@IsEmpty = IsEmpty FROM TrolleyMaster 
	WHERE TrolleyNo = @TrolleyNo

	If(@PackSize = 0)
	Begin
		Select 'Wrong Trolly No' As Result
	End
	Else If(@IsEmpty = 'False')
	Begin
		Select 'Trolley is already full' As Result
	End
	Else
	Begin
		Select 'Y' As Result,@PackQty As PackQty,@PackSize As PackSize
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [dbo].[test]    Script Date: 28-10-2020 10:58:25 AM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE proc [dbo].[test]
As
begin
	Begin Try
	declare @id int =0,@id2 int=5,@id3 int
	set @id3 = @id2/@id
	select 'Y'
	End Try
	Begin Catch
		--Throw 
		 DECLARE @ErrorMessage NVARCHAR(4000);  
    DECLARE @ErrorSeverity INT;  
    DECLARE @ErrorState INT;  
  
    SELECT   
        @ErrorMessage = ERROR_MESSAGE(),  
        @ErrorSeverity = ERROR_SEVERITY(),  
        @ErrorState = ERROR_STATE();  
  
    -- Use RAISERROR inside the CATCH block to return error  
    -- information about the original error that caused  
    -- execution to jump to the CATCH block.  
    RAISERROR (@ErrorMessage, -- Message text.  
               @ErrorSeverity, -- Severity.  
               @ErrorState -- State.  
               );
	End Catch
end
